<p>213a.7</p>la dbang bskur ba'i bum pa ni/ ras kyis mgul ba bcings pa bdud rtsi lnga dang gser dang dngul dang / mu tig dang / byi ru dag dang dung ste rin po che lnga dang / thabs kyi sman lnga shes rab kyi sman lnga ste bcu dang / ga bur dang tsan+dan la sogs pa dri'i bye brag dang / ar+g+ha'i snod
<p>213b</p>
<p>213b.1</p>tsu ta'i shing dang / tsam pa ka'i yan lag dang ldan pa dang / bum pa'i nang du thabs kyi sman am+bu tsam+bu dang / ka dam+pa dang / bilba dang / bI dza pU ra dang / ba la mo ta dang / drug pa ni dany+dza dany+dza dang / bdun pa ke ri karni ka dang / brgyad pa e na ra bi da dang / dgu pa ha sa de ba dang / 
<p>213b.2</p>bcu pa tsam bu ste sman rnams bum par bcug la/ sku'i sman i ma na dang / gsung gi sman dzA ti pha la dang / thugs kyi sman gla gor zho sha dang bcas pas sku khrus gsol ba dang dbang bskur ro/ /chu'i dbang bskur ba'i rjes la gser gyi mchod phyir thogs cod pan dang bcas pa
<p>213b.3</p>dang phyag rgya drug gis brgyan nas/ lha la na bza' gsol te/ sgrub pa po rnams rnam par rtog pa med pa'i sems gcer bus gar byed cing stong pa nyid kyi sems kyis rab gnas byas pa'i lha la dad pa sngon du 'gro bas dus gsum du mchod pa'am/ tshes bcu'am yar ngo mar ngo'i
<p>213b.4</p>tshes bco lnga la mchod par bya'o/ /go cha bskon pa dang / ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myang ba dang / spyan dbye ba rna ba dang sna dang zhal dbye ba na bza' gsol la yo byad dbul/ de nas mchod pa rgyas pa bya ba kha bskang ngo / /le'u bzhi
<p>213b.5</p>bcu rtsa brgyad pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de ltar rab gnas bshad nas dbang bskur ba'i 'khor lo 'chad pa ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ dkyil 'khor thams cad du dngos grub bsgrub pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi le'u dang po ro mnyam gyi dkyil 'khor
<p>213b.6</p>dam pa 'dir dbang bskur bas/ dkyil 'khor gyi snying po lha thams cad skyes pa'i le'u 'dis bsdus pa yin no/ /de ltar mdor bstan nas rgyas par bshad pa ni/ /shin du mnyam gzhag sgrub pa pos/ /zhes pa tshigs bcad gcig gis rten gyi gang zag bstan to/ /sprang
<p>213b.7</p>mi mtshal dang ga bur bcas/ /zhes bya bas gsang ba'i dbang bskur ba dngos te sbrang rtsi ni mi bskyod pa'o/ /mtshal ni rang 'byung ngo / /ga bur ni byang sems so/ /tsan+dan dmar ni sha chen no/ /sbyar ba ni rnam par snang mdzad dang go cha'i lha'i rigs tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i nang
<p>214a</p>
<p>214a.1</p>du bum pa bzhi'i gnas su bzhag nas/ kha zas kun gyi mchog tu bcud kyis len du 'gyur ro/ /tshogs kyi lha de rnams ji lta bu zhe na/ rdo rje kun 'khor dang mchog gtso bo mtshan ma thams cad rdo rje'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'o/ /bcud len du ji ltar 'gyur zhe na/ 
<p>214a.2</p>oM AHhUM gsum gyis byin gyis brlabs nas/ grol ba'i lam pas sbom po mtheb mo dang / mtha' ltag srin lag gi rtse mo sbyar nas rnal 'byor pas sgyu ma lta bu rig pas btung bar bya'o/ /chags lam gyi dbang du byas nas/ rdo rje gdan bzhi las sbom po mtha' ltag b+ha ga
<p>214a.3</p>rtse sbyar ba a wa d+hU tI ra phrad nas bde ba sgyu ma lta bur rig pas rtag tu spyad pa'o/ /rnal 'byor pa gnyi ga la mtshungs pa de ma thag pa'i rkyen srog /a wa d+hU tIr sod pa dang dbang po bdag po'i rkyen bsam gtan thob nas chags lam grol lam gnyi ga /yul ro dang reg bya yin
<p>214a.4</p>pas sgyu mar 'gro ba the tshom med do/ /dper na mu stegs can la ri bo ba di ra las rtswa so ma na btus nas wA rA Na sI'i bya ka ra gi wang yod pa'i ba ser mo'i pags par btums nas rig byed kyi sngags kyis byin gyis brlabs nas gang zag gis 'thungs pas srid pa'i ting nge
<p>214a.5</p>'dzin thob pa'i dpe de bzhin du/ bdud rtsi lnga myangs na dngos grub rtag pa 'dus ma byas 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /gal te sgyu ma lta bu ma rtogs na mi 'chi bar tshe ring ba dang nad med par 'gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi dngos grub thams cad la 'jug go/ /de ltar zhi ba'i btung ba sgyu ma
<p>214a.6</p>lta bur rtogs nas sngags 'bum bzlas na dkyil 'khor byar rung / gnyis pa shes rab ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba mchod pa bzhi rdo rje'i rigs la stong nyid bsgom pa dang / rin po che'i rigs la mtshan ma med pa dang / pad+ma'i rigs la smon pa med pa dang / las kyi rigs la 'od gsal
<p>214a.7</p>ba'i mchod pa bzhi ye shes las skyes pa bsgom pa de bzhin du/ dpa' bo rnal 'byor pa ni las dang po pa'i ngan par spyod pa la yang dbang po gnyis kyi a wa d+hU tI'i reg bya las don dam pa'i de kho na nyid 'dus ma byas sems kyis 'dzin cing rtogs pa ni bsnyen pa yin no/ /des kyang
<p>214b</p>
<p>214b.1</p>gtso bo la 'bum dang me tog phog pa'i lha la 'bum/ 'khor la khri bzla'o/ /bde ba stong pa nyid de lha dang mi'i bde ba zag bcas pas zag med kyi bcu drug char yang mi phod do zhes rtsa ba'i rgyud las gsungs te/ 'dir zag med las byung ba'i dkyil 'khor la yang brtags nas bshad do/ /
<p>214b.2</p>bsnyen pa bstan nas sa'i cho ga'i dkyil 'khor gyi gnas bshad pa gdod nas grub pa'i dur khrod la sogs par dkyil 'khor brtsam par bya zhes bya ba sa'i cho ga go sla'o/ /dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshon nyid ni gdul bya drag po 'jigs byed dur khrod du spyod pa dang mthun pa'i ro
<p>214b.3</p>bsregs pa'i sol ba'i phye ma las nag po rus phye la dkar po/ so phag tshig pa las dmar po/ ma tshig pa las ser po/ dur khrod shing lo las ljang gu bya ste/ phyug na rin po che dang bsre/ dbul na rin po che med pa'o/ /tshon gyi mtshan nyid bshad nas bzhi pa slob dpon gyi mtshan
<p>214b.4</p>nyid ni/ lus ngag yid gsum thams cad zag med dang ldan pa'o/ /zag bcas kyi mtshan nyid kun spangs pa/ sems kyi mtshan nyid ni rgyud sde bzhi 'dus ma byas zhes pa ni 'dus byas lha'i 'khor lo shes pa/ sngags zhes pa ni ngag go/ /khro med snying rje can gtsang ba/ ltung ba med
<p>214b.5</p>pa mkhas pa de nyid bcu shes pa sbyor zhes zhi gnas dang ldan pa ye shes lhag mthong gis 'khor ba'i pha rol tu 'gro ba spyi gtsug rus pa'i 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pas brgyan pa nas phyag rgya drug la thal bas byugs pa/ go cha drug gis lus brgyan pa rus pa'i phreng ba'i tshangs pa'i
<p>214b.6</p>skud pa can rna rgyan la sogs pa rus dang ldan pa dum bu gcig las spyi gtsug gi 'khor lo byas pa/ rus phreng gi do shal yod pa lag pa g.yon pas kha T+wAM ga gzung ba/ g.yas pas cang te'u thogs pa/ gnas dang ldang ba nyid dang ni/ /'jug dang yongs su rdzogs pa dang / byin
<p>214b.7</p>gyis brlab dang dbang bskur dang / ting 'dzin mchod pa nye bar bsdu/ /zhes bya ba'i bar gyis sta gon gyi lha bsgoms pas bdag nyid he ru kar byas nas/ de'i 'og tu bgegs nye bar zhi ba'i cho ga byed pas/ snying gar 'khor lo nyi shu la bcug nas bdag nyid go cha chen po lus kyi
<p>215a</p>
<p>215a.1</p>'khor lo la bgos te ra ba rnams phyogs bzhir dgod/ 'og tu sna tshogs rdo rje'i 'khor lo'i gzhal yas khang dang 'dra ba steng du mda'i dra ba bdag nyid la go cha drug bskon/ logs su rdo rje'i ra ba steng du rdo rje'i bla re me 'od kyi phreng ba phur bus gdab pa byas na sum cu rtsa
<p>215a.2</p>gsum gyi lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis kyang gzhig par mi nus phan yon no/ /de nas lha lhag gnas/ bum pa sbyin sreg /slob ma lhag gnas kha bskang de ltar sta gon rdzogs nas bdag nyid la sngags go cha drug dang / phyag rgya drug gis brgyan pa'i lhar bskyed nas/ dkyil 'khor 'jigs
<p>215a.3</p>pa bri bar bya/ /zhes pa ni mdor bstan to/ /rgyas bshad ni de nas sems med ro'i skra'am/ rgyus pa'am/ ro g.yogs kyi ras kyi skud pas thig gdab pa ni go sla'o/ /de'i dbus su tshon dgye ba ni/ pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad pa lte ba dang ge sar du bcas pa'i steng du bcom ldan 'das
<p>215a.4</p>zhal bzhi spyan gsum phyag bcu gnyis las glang po che'i pags pa smin mtshams kyi thad du bsnams pa/ rdo rje dang dril bu 'gying bas snying gar 'khyud pa/ kha T+wAM ga dang phyag mtshan lnga bstan pas phyag mtshan bdun le'u bcu bzhi pa ro mnyam gyi 'khor lo las shes so/ /lhag ma ni
<p>215a.5</p>go sla'o/ /dpa' bo dang dpa' mo drug cu yang ro mnyam bzhin du sku mdog dang phyag mtshan bya'o/ /dngos grub 'dod na lha yab yum tshang pa la dbang bskur bya ma tshang na dngos grub mi thob bo/ /thig gdab pa dang tshon dgye ba bstan nas bum pa bsgrub pa ni/ rtsa ba nag po med pa mtshan
<p>215a.6</p>nyid do/ /mu tig la sogs pa ni rin po che lnga'o/ /grangs shar phyogs su rgyal ba dang bkra shis/ /lho phyogs su dngos grub dang rnam 'phrul/ nub tu rgyal ba dang rnam rgyal/ byang du grub pa dang srung ba/ rnam rgyal dang grub pa la gser dngul gyis phyag mtshan bris la mu tig gi
<p>215a.7</p>phreng bas kha brgyan pa'o/ /de ltar bum pa bsgrub pa bshad nas/ dkyil 'khor gyi yo byad ni/ dkyil 'khor thams cad 'byor na rin po che gser la sogs pas bris na dngos grub thob bo/ /kun nas sgo'i bum pa las thams cad rnam par rgyal ba'i dri'i chus bsang la/ mar
<p>215b</p>
<p>215b.1</p>me zhes bya ba sems gsal bar byed pa'i sha rgyas nye bar mtshon pa'i me tog bdug pa mar me dri chab lha bshos kun rgyan yin no/ /de ltar rdzas bsags nas don lnga pa ye shes sems dpa' spyan drang ba ni/ mkha' 'gro ma yid la gzhug pa dang / sa stengs gsung la gzhug pa dang / sa
<p>215b.2</p>'og sku la gzhug pa dang / ma mo bcu gnyis phyogs mtshams su gzhug pa dang / dur khrod brgyad dang gzhal yas khang yang shugs kyis rtogs so/ /don drug pa mchod pa'i rdzas dbul ba ni/ dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma re re la dngos grub 'dod pas mchod par bya'o/ /rgyal mtshan
<p>215b.3</p>ni go sla'o/ /dmar ba gsung dang ser ba ye shes kyi 'khor la dkar ba sku/ gnag pa dang thugs/ ser skya sgo bzhi la/ sna tshogs pa mtshams bzhi la mda' dang phur bu brgyad kyis bsrung ba dang / bza' ba dang btung ba tshogs 'khor la'o/ /de ltar drug pas dkyil 'khor mchod nas/ 
<p>215b.4</p>slob mas 'dod yon lnga'i dngos po kun gyis slob dpon mnyes par byas la/ dngos grub 'dod pas ci nus kyi yon dbul lo/ /de nas slob dpon gyi bdag 'jug bya ste/ dril sbyang lo bcu gnyis ma dang ting nge 'dzin bsgom pa dang / sgra snyan dril bu bcu drug ma dang bsgom pa dang / brda nyi shu
<p>215b.5</p>pa dang ting nge 'dzin bsgom pa ha brgyad kyis ye shes bab kyi bar du bsgom la de nyid kyi dga' bral du mi gtang bar bya'o/ /de ltar slob ma'i gdong la dar gyis bcings nas/ snyim par me tog gzhag pa phyi'i 'jug pa bdun rnam par dag pa dang / sdom pa gzung ba dang / byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / 
<p>215b.6</p>lhar bskyed pa dang / phyi rol bum pa'i chus dbang bskur ba dang / sgo bzhi nas zhugs nas pad+ma'i gar bskor bas phyag bya ba dang / slob ma sras por lha'i dam tshig bsgrags pa dang / slob dpon gyi dam tshig bsgrags pa dang / ye shes dbab pa dang / snyim pa'i me tog gtor ba/ 
<p>215b.7</p>gang du babs pa rang gi lhar shes par bya ba'i phyir lan cig bskor ba byas nas shin tu mnyam par bzhag pas ye shes dbab pa dang / grong khyer mchog gi nang du gzhug pa'o/ /de nas slob mas lho phyogs su lus kyis gnas te sngar me tog 'phangs pa ma phog na slar yang snyim
<p>216a</p>
<p>216a.1</p>pas dor te/ gang la bab pa de'i rigs bstan/ gdong g.yogs bkrol/ dkyil 'khor bstan/ dbab pa nye bar bsdu ba bya/ lha de'i ming gis gdags/ de ltar 'jug pa rdzogs nas/ slob dpon legs par mnyam par bzhag pas phyag rgya lha mo rnams
<p>216a.2</p>ye shes phab nas bum pa dang / cod pan dang / rdo rje dang / dril bu dang / ming gis dbang bskur la/ de nas nyin zhag gnyis pa la sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud las bdud rtsi lnga la mtshal chen gyi ming gis btags pa la/ oM AHhUM gsum gyi bzlas pas gnas gsum
<p>216a.3</p>du thig le byas la/ lce la bdud rtsi lnga bzhag nas gsang ba'i dbang bskur bar bya'o/ de nas nyin zhag gsum pa la slob ma'i gdong phye la lus kyi dkyil 'khor bstan nas/ bde ba stong pa nyid bskyed pa'i lha'i gnas rtsa dbu ma gang yin pa der 'dus ma byas kyi stong nyid de yang
<p>216a.4</p>bstan par bya'o/ /de ltar shes rab ye shes kyi dbang bskur nas slob mas slob dpon la phyag bya bskor ba bya/ yon dbul ba ni go sla'o/ /de ltar bla ma nyes pa dang / dbang bskur ba nges par byas nas de'i rjes la sgrub pa pos yon dbul ba rab tu nges par bya'o/ /de ltar byas
<p>216a.5</p>pa'i phan yon ni/ /sgrub pa po de la mkha' 'gro ma kun mnyes pas sgrub pa po'i mngag gzhug byed pa dang po'o/ /rnal 'byor pa la dngos grub tu 'gyur ba mi snang ba gnyis so/ /sgrub pa po rang 'dod pa tsam gyis gzugs du ma byed pa dang / tshar gcod pa dang phan 'dogs pa
<p>216a.6</p>gsum pa'o/ /sngags pa dkyil 'khor ma mthong bas dngos grub mi 'thob pa dang / sku gsum gyi dkyil 'khor 'dir dbang bskur na lha la sogs pa zil gyis gnon pa dang / de nyid bsdus pa la sogs pa las khyad par du 'gyur ba ston to/ /de ltar phan yon lnga bshad nas/ 
<p>216a.7</p>'di'i brjod bya bshad zin pa'i don dang ma bshad pa'i don thams cad kyis brjod bya dang / dpal he ru ka'i snang ba yin par ston to/ /le'u bzhi bcu rtsa dgu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de ltar dbang bskur ba'i 'khor lo bshad nas/ bstod pa 'chad pa ni/ de nas gzhan yang
<p>216b</p>
<p>216b.1</p>bshad bya ba/ /zhes gsungs te/ chags pa dang bcas pa dang / chags bral gyi mtshams gang du chags bral gyi chus mi gos shing 'dod pa'i khams kyi chags pa spangs pa'i mtshams der stong pa nyid kyis rgyas btab nas/ sems can thams cad kyi srid pa 'jig par
<p>216b.2</p>byed pa'o/ /de ltar mdor bstan nas rgyas par bshad pa ni gong du bstan pa'i rim pas sngon 'gro'i rnal 'byor lnga dang / dngos gzhi 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rje dang bcas pa bskyed nas/ he ru ka dbyangs skyong gi lha mngon par byang chub lnga'i rim pas rdzus skyes cig car
<p>216b.3</p>'byung ba'i snang ba bsgom mo/ /de yang / /dung kun da'i mdog kyang 'dzin/ /zhes bya ba nas/ thun bzhi ru ni bsgrub par bya/ /zhes bya ba go sla'o/ /zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sku mdog dkar po dbyangs skyong gi lha bsgoms nas/ dbyangs skyong gi bstod pa'i don ni rnal 'byor pas
<p>216b.4</p>lha thams cad bsgom pa la dga' bral/ 'dod pa'i khams kyi sems su mi gtong zhes bstod pa yin no/ /de la rdzogs rim bsgom pa ni/ dga' ba bzhi'i gnas 'khor lo bzhi dang a thung dang haM las bden pa bzhi dang phag mo dang khrag 'thung ba'i ming gis btags pa la rtsa
<p>216b.5</p>'dab drug cu rtsa bzhi dang brgyad dang bcu drug dang sum cu rtsa gnyis pa dag la dga' bral du mi 'gyur ba'i lam bde ba chen po stong pa nyid bsgom pa la dbyangs skyong zhes bya'o/ /de ltar rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i mtshams su/ rjes su sgrub pa'i don bskyed pa'i rim pas zhal gsum phyag drug
<p>216b.6</p>pa'i lha'i sku bsgoms nas bdud rtsi lnga myangs te dbyangs skyong gi sngags kyis mnyam par bzhag pas bzlas pa bya'o/ /de la ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / go cha bgo ba dang dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myangs nas bsgom pa dang / bzlas par bya ba shes so/ /de la dbyangs
<p>216b.7</p>skyong gi 'bras bu dang po phrin las rnam bzhi kun byed pa gnyis pa dus ma yin pa'i 'chi ba las rgyal ba/ gsum pa zhi ba la sogs pa 'grub pa/ bzhi pa dus gsum shes pa/ lnga pa stong phrag gcig bzlas pas 'jig rten gsum gyi dngos grub thob pa/ drug pa zhag gsum gyis lha'i
<p>217a</p>
<p>217a.1</p>'khor los sgyur ba thob pa/ bdun pa mngon shes drug rig pa/ brgyad pa skye rga na 'chi spangs pa'o/ /de ltar 'bras bu bshad nas/ gal te de ma thob na bskyar ba'i cho ga ni/ 'byung po'i nyin zhag gsum la tshogs 'khor byas la ye shes sems dpa' spyan drang / gal
<p>217a.2</p>te mngon sum mthong na phyag bya mchod yon dbul/ 'dod pa'i don la gsol ba btab nas dngos grub blang / mngon par shes pa drug mnga' ba'i dpa' bo thams cad mkhyen pa khams gsum gyi mchog tu 'gyur ro/ /de'i phan yon ni/ 'di ni dpa' bo chen po ste/ gnyis pa
<p>217a.3</p>thams cad rnam par spangs/ /zhes pa bdag lta'i gzung 'dzin dang bral nas sa gzhi rgya mtsho dang bcas pa'i 'gro ba rigs drug gi don la dbang bar 'gyur ro/ /dkyil 'khor gyi bstod pa mngon par brjod pa le'u lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang bshad pa ni/ 
<p>217a.4</p>dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi nye ba'i snying po yi ge bdun pa'i lha bsgom pa ni gong du bstan pa'i sngon 'gro lnga byas nas 'byung ba bzhi dang ri rab sna tshogs rdo rjer gyur pa'i rang bzhin gzhal yas khang gi dbus su yi ge hUM las byung ba'i rdo rje mkha' 'gro zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sku mdog
<p>217a.5</p>dang phyag mtshan go sla'o/ /lha mo drug ni hUM dang phaT kyi bar du yi ge drug las bskyed do/ /ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / go cha bskon pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myang ba dang / byang chub yan lag bdun bsgom pa dang bzlas pa ni snga ma bzhin shes par bya'o/ /
<p>217a.6</p>khro bo kun gyi gnas mchog ste/ /mnyam med gsang sngags bzla bar bya/ /zhes bya ba'i 'khor lo rtsibs drug pa bkod pa de la yi ge bdun pa bkod nas bzlas na zhag bdun gyis the tshom med par 'grub ste nA ro pas dgyes pa'i rdo rje yan lag drug gis 'chad pa'i 'grel
<p>217a.7</p>pa mdzad nas mtshan thog thag gcig gis ti lo pa'i lung bstan thob pa'i phyir te/ gdams ngag drug 'grub nas shAn+ti pa las gsang 'dus zhus/ he badzra'i 'grel pa mtha' drug tshul bzhi pa mdzad do/ /ma grub na bskyar ba'i cho ga ni/ dpyi zla tha chungs kyi nya la tshogs
<p>217b</p>
<p>217b.1</p>kyi 'khor lo byas na tho rangs he ru ka dang mtshungs par 'gyur ro/ /mngon par brjod pa las le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi snying po bshad pa ni/ sngon 'gro lnga 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rje dang gzhal yas khang bskyed la/ 
<p>217b.2</p>de'i dbus su yi ge nyi shu rtsa gcig las drod gsher skyes kyi lha sems can kun la phan 'dogs pa bskyed de/ hUM dang shrI gnyis gtso bo yab yum zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'o/ /pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad la oM shar du/ ba byang du/ dzra nub tu/ he lho ru/ de las
<p>217b.3</p>'khor mkha' 'gro ma bzhi zhal gsum phyag drug pa'o/ /mtshams bzhi ru bum pa bzhi dang thod pa/ shar la sogs pa'i rtsibs brgyad zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa mdog sngon po sha stag go/ /sgo bzhi dang mtshams bzhir lha mo brgyad zhal gsum phyag drug pa'o/ /sku mdog dang phyag
<p>217b.4</p>mtshan rgyud las go sla'o/ /ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / go cha bskon pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myang ba dang / bsgom pa'i tshe dpral bar sku'i 'khor lo/ lkog mar gsung gi 'khor lo/ snying gar thugs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor bas spro bsdu bsgoms la/ lha nyi shu rtsa gnyis
<p>217b.5</p>po thams cad kyi snying po/ oM shri badzra he he ru ru kaM hUM hUM phaT DA ki nI dz+wA la sam+ba raM swA hA zhes bzla bar bya'o/ /gal te rnam dag bsgoms na zhal brgyad rnam thar brgyad phyag bcu drug stong nyid bcu drug /nang gi yum bzhi so sor yang dag par rig pa bzhi/ 'khor lo rtsibs kyi phyogs bzhir lha
<p>217b.6</p>mo ston pa bzhi/ mtshams bzhi'i lha mo chos kyi mdo bzhi/ phyi rol gyi sgo bzhi dang mtshams bzhi mi 'jigs pa bzhi'o/ /dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu kA li nyi ma las bcom ldan 'das skyes/ dbyangs yig sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi rang bzhin las yum skyes par bsgom mo/ /mchod pa dang
<p>217b.7</p>bstod pa dang / gtor ma gtang ba dang / nye bar bsdu ba kha bskang ngo / /le'u lnga bcu rtsa gnyis pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rnam par bshad pa ni gsum du 'gyur te/ srog a wa d+hU tIr chud nas gtum mo drod kyis byang chub kyi sems
<p>218a</p>
<p>218a.1</p>phab pa ye shes lnga'i rang bzhin/ sku'i rang bzhin sa'i cha ni spyan du snang / rtsa 'khor lo'i char phye ba thig skud rnam snang du snang / khams nyi shu rtsa bzhi rdul tshon sna tshogs dang mchod pa sna tshogs su snang / mgo bo pul+lI ra mA la'i rlung lte ba'i pad+ma brgyad du snang / spyi gtsug dzA
<p>218a.2</p>lan+d+ha ra'i rlung thugs kyi 'khor lor snang / rna ba g.yas pa o D+ya na gyi rlung gsung gi 'khor lor snang / rtag pa arbu da'i rlung sku'i 'khor lor snang / rna ba g.yon pa go dA ba ri'i rlung logs bzhir snang / smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu'i rlung shar lho mtshams su snang / mig de bI ko TI
<p>218a.3</p>rlung bden bral mtshams su snang / phrag pa mA la be'i rlung nub byang gi zur du snang / mchan khung kA ma rU pa'i rlung dbang ldan gyi zur du snang / nu ma o Te'i rlung shar sgor snang / lte ba tri sha ku ni'i rlung lho sgor snang / sna rtse ko sa la'i rlung nub sgor snang / kha ka ling+ga'i rlung byang sgor snang / mid
<p>218a.4</p>pa lam+pa ka'i rlung shar gyi rta babs su snang / snying ga kAny+tsi'i rlung lho'i rta babs su snang / rgyu zhabs kyi hi ma la'i rlung nub kyi rta babs su snang / gsang ba'i gnas pre ta pu ri'i rlung byang gi rta babs su snang / gr-i ha de ba ta'i rlung lha'i snam bur snang / brla sau rASh+Ta'i rlung rin chen pha gur snang / 
<p>218a.5</p>byin pa gser gyi gling rlung dra ba dra phyed du snang / sor mo nA ga ra'i rlung rnga yab la sogs par snang / rkang po la sin+d+hU'i rlung rdo rje'i thig zlum por snang / rkang pa'i mtheb mo ma ro'i rlung sgo khyud bzhir snang ngo / /pus mo ku lu tA'i rlung zur rnams kyi rdo rje rin po cher snang / de ltar pad+ma dkar po
<p>218a.6</p>lta bu'i gang zag gcig srog a wa d+hU tIr chud nas bde ba stong pa nyid skyes pa'i snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lor snang / gsang ba sngags su bshad pa'i gsung gi rnam dag go/ /gtum mo drod spar nas/ byang chub sems ni sum cu gnyis/ /gang tshe 'dir ni yongs gang ba/ /
<p>218a.7</p>de tshe lus kyi dkyil 'khor yin/ /zhes gsungs pas/ ut+pal lta bu'i gang zag lus byang chub sems kyis gang ba'i rkang pa dang lag pa don yod grub pa'i snang ba dkyil 'khor gyi nang khong stong kun du snang ngo / /dpral ba'i snang ba sku'i 'khor lo/ lkog ma'i snang ba gsung gi
<p>218b</p>
<p>218b.1</p>'khor lo/ /snying ga'i snang ba thugs kyi 'khor lo/ lte ba'i snang ba dbus kyi pad+ma sgo bzhi dang rta babs dang dur khrod la sogs pa rnams su snang ngo / /lus kyi tshor ba bde ba rtog med kyi snang ba sku'i 'khor lo/ /'du shes bde ba rtog med gsung gi 'khor lo/ 'du byed bde ba rtog
<p>218b.2</p>med thugs kyi 'khor lo/ rnam shes bde ba rtog med nang gi pad+ma 'dab brgyad shin tu rnam par dag pas ye shes ri mo lngar snang / khams kyi dpa' bo nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i snang ba pany+tsa rA ga phyogs bzhi'i nyi shu/ sa gzhi'i kha dog bzhi dang nyi shu rtsa bzhir snang ngo / /nyi shu rtsa bzhi ni
<p>218b.3</p>rnal 'byor ma 'khor lo'i rtsibs nyi shu rtsa bzhir snang ngo / /lte ba khung gi thig le rdo rje phag mor snang ngo / /snying ga'i byang chub sems kyi sa bon khrag 'thung mchog tu snang ngo / /snying ga'i rtsa bzhi'i rang bzhin mkha' 'gro ma bzhir snang ngo / /de ltar na dman pa dbyibs su bshad pa rtsa dang
<p>218b.4</p>khams kyi bde ba las skyes pa'i snang ba yin te/ sems can la snang ba'i dkyil 'khor 'bras bu yin la/ de'i rgyu gsang sngags rlung las bde ba skyes pa'i snang ba'am/ dman pa dbyibs rtsa la bde ba skyes pa'i snang ba bshad pa yin no/ /mthar thug chos su byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos
<p>218b.5</p>sum cu rtsa bdun rin po che lta bu'i gang zag mthar thug chos bsgom pa ni/ dpa' bo dang dpa' mo ltar snang ba'o/ /lha de yang yig 'bru'i dkyil 'khor dang / phyag mtshan gyi dkyil 'khor la sogs pa drug tu snang ste go sla'o/ /mthar thug chos sems dang sbyar na/ dbus kyi pad+ma sa dang
<p>218b.6</p>po rab tu dga' ba'i snang ba nas/ rta babs chos kyi sprin gyi snang ba las dngos grub rgya che ba thob par 'gyur ba ni go sla'o/ /de ltar na rnam dag bshad nas/ de kho na nyid bzhi bshad pa'i dang po 'khor lo bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor la shes rab ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba'i b+ha ga'i dkyil
<p>218b.7</p>'khor dang / gsang ba'i dbang bskur ba'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor dang / dbang bzhi pa bskur ba'i rin chen sems kyi stong nyid gnyis med kha sbyar gyi dkyil 'khor dang gsum yin no/ /dang po dkyil 'khor gyi de nyid bshad nas/ gnyis pa bdag gi de nyid ni gtso bo'i lha'i ting nge 'dzin yin
<p>219a</p>
<p>219a.1</p>no/ /gsum pa lha'i de nyid ni 'khor gyi ting nge 'dzin yin no/ /sngags kyi de nyid ni phyag rgya stang stabs sngags zlos pa'o/ /de ltar na de nyid bzhi yin no/ /dkyil 'khor gyi mjug bsdu ba ni/ sgo bzhi dang mtshams bzhi dang / rta babs bzhi la sogs pa'i yul gyi yan lag kun
<p>219a.2</p>las 'das pas zhes pa rtog bcas dang / rtog med spangs pa brjod phyi mo thig le las 'das pa ni 'dus ma byas kyi dkyil 'khor de mchog yin no/ /de la lus kyi dkyil 'khor ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas/ lus kyi rtog pa chos dge mi dge sgyu ma lta bur rnam par spyod pa rten dang brten
<p>219a.3</p>pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par dag pa khams nam mkha'i 'ja' tshon dang mtshungs pa ni bdag byin gyis rlob pa'i dkyil 'khor ro/ /gnyis pa dkyil 'khor b+ha ga ni 'khor ba'i chags pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i chags med du mnyam pa pad+ma rA gas kha bsgyur ba'i chu
<p>219a.4</p>bzhin du rang gi sems kyi chos nyid bde bas kha bsgyur ba bde ba stong nyid kyi dkyil 'khor gyi mchog yin no/ /gsum pa chos kyi 'khor lo ni/ 'dod khams gnas rigs nyi shu gzugs khams gnas rigs bcu bdun gzugs med skye mched mu bzhi las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor
<p>219a.5</p>te/ ming gsum ni go sla'o/ /le'u lnga bcu rtsa gsum pa'i 'grel pa'o// //dkyil 'khor thams cad la mtshan ma thob na tshogs kyi 'khor lo ji lta bu snyam na/ de nas gsang ba bshad bya ba/ /zhes gsungs te/ sems can mtshan ma thob pa thams cad la phan pa'i dngos grub
<p>219a.6</p>gsol ba A li kA li mngon par byang chub pa lnga las chos kyi dbyings kyi grong khyer dang bcas pa cig car rdzus skyes byed pa'o/ /de ltar mdor bstan bshad nas rgyas par bshad pa ni/ rnal 'byor pho mo 'tshogs nas sngon 'gro tshogs sogs pa lnga dang / 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs
<p>219a.7</p>rdo rje pad+ma dang bcas pa bskyed la/ de'i lte ba'i dbus su mngon par byang chub pa lnga'i rim pas gzhal yas khang dang bcas pa dus gcig la bskyed la/ dbus su pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad la ye shes kyi 'khor lo nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du thugs kyi 'khor lo brgyad/ gtso bo zhal
<p>219b</p>
<p>219b.1</p>bzhi phyag brgyad pa/ lha mo yang zhal bzhi phyag brgyad pa/ ye shes kyi lha mo bzhi dang / thugs kyi 'khor lo brgyad sngar gang la mtshan ma thob pa'i lha'i sku mdog dang phyag mtshan de bzhin du bsgom mo/ thugs kyi 'khor lo'i phyi rgyab tu gsung gi 'khor lo shar dang / byang du dmar po
<p>219b.2</p>rtsibs brgyad nub dang / lho ru dkar po rtsibs brgyad pa/ mtshams su gshin rje brtan ma la sogs pa/ sgor khwa gdong ma la sogs pa ye shes kyi lha yab yum gdong rgyan can lha mo bcu gnyis thams cad shar sngo ba/ rams sam mthing shun gyis byugs pa/ byang thams cad
<p>219b.3</p>spang mas byugs pa/ nub mtshal gyis byugs pa/ lhor ba blas byugs pa/ phyogs bzhi'i kha dog can de bzhin du thugs kun la rams kyis byugs pa nag po/ gsung mtshal gyis byugs pa/ sku rdo thal gyis byugs pa ji ltar 'dod pa'i khyad par rdo rje snying pos bshad pa'i
<p>219b.4</p>gnas nyi shu rtsa bzhir dpa' bor mos na rnal 'byor pa nyi tshe'i bya'o/ /kha cig dpa' mo la mos na rnal 'byor ma nyi tshe bya/ sngar bshad pa'i kha dog dang dbyibs dang spyod lam sna tshogs pas rigs ji ltar 'dod pa bsgom/ gzhan yang zhal dang phyag mtshan ni sngar bshad pa bzhin
<p>219b.5</p>du gnas kyi rim pas dgod do/ /de la yang ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa/ go cha bskon pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / sum cu rtsa bdun gyi rnam dag bsgom pa dang bzlas pa bya'o/ /A li kA li las byung ba bsgom pa dga' ba/ rnam par bsgom
<p>219b.6</p>pa mchog dga'/ bsgom pa lhan cig skyes dga'/ mchog 'od gsal ba dga' ba bzhi bsgom par bya'o/ /chos kyi dbyings kyi grong khyer rnam par dag pa 'di ni rdul tshon dang lugs su blugs pa dang / 'bur du brkos pa dang / ri mor bris pa ma yin te/ sngar bshad pa'i
<p>219b.7</p>mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i sems can gyi khams rab tu bcug nas gsang ba'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo 'di su la yang mi bstan to/ /le'u lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang shes rab kyi tshogs 'khor bshad par bya ba ni/ b+ha ga'i pad+ma shes rab la
<p>220a</p>
<p>220a.1</p>mos pa bsgom pa rdo rje snying pos zhus pa la bka' stsal pa ni/ shes rab kyi tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni nges par gsang ba'o/ /rnal 'byor pho mo 'tshogs nas sngon 'gro lnga bsgom/ 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rje pad+ma 'dab ma gsum pa bskyed/ de'i dbus su mngon
<p>220a.2</p>par byang chub pa lnga'i rim pas rdo rje phag mo dang he ru ka ma'i slob dpon lte ba la bsgom/ gzhal yas khang dang bcas pa rdzus skyes kyi 'dab ma gsum la ye shes kyi lha mo mkha' 'gro ma lA ma dum skyes ma gsum bsgom/ bcom ldan 'das dang lha mo rnams kyi sku mdog dang phyag mtshan rgyud na
<p>220a.3</p>gsal/ gru gsum gyi pad+ma'i phyi rol du thugs kyi 'khor lo'i lha brgyad dgod/ dbus kyi pad+ma'i logs gsum du thod pa gsum dang bum pa gsum gzhag /dkyil 'khor gyi zur gsum gyi shar gyi zur la sku'i 'khor lo brgyad/ nub byang gi zur la dam tshig gi 'khor lo brgyad/ 
<p>220a.4</p>lho nub mtshams su gsung gi 'khor lo brgyad/ /bcom ldan 'das zhal bzhi phyag bzhi pa'i sku mdog dang phyag mtshan ni rgyud na gsal/ ye shes dang thugs dang gsung dang sku'i 'khor lo dam tshig gi 'khor lo rnal 'byor pho mo gang mos pa'i sku mdog dang phyag mtshan can bsgoms te/ 
<p>220a.5</p>thams cad rang gi cod pan can/ /zhes bya ba'i bar ni rgyud kyis gsal lo/ /dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma de dag mkha' 'gro bla ma'i brgyud pa'i rim pas lus kyi dkyil 'khor bsgom pa dang / go cha dgod pa dang / ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / sku gsung thugs lha'i 'khor
<p>220a.6</p>lo spro bsdu dang / rang rang gi bzlas pa ni rnal 'byor ma ye shes babs pa'i zhal brgyad pa'i rim pa la mnyam par gzhag cing rtag tu bsgom mo/ /'di su la yang mi bstan/ su'i rna bar yang ma brjod na dpa' bo dang gnyis su med pas dngos grub 'thob bo /dam tshig rtag tu
<p>220a.7</p>bsrung bya zhing / /bza' dang bca' ba spyad par bya/ /zhes bya ba ni tshogs kyi 'khor lo la bya ste/ rang gi lha mo bgrod min gzhan gyi lha mo la dus bzhir gtum mo drod dang byang chub sems 'char nub bsten na sngags 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /le'u lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa'i 'grel
<p>220b</p>
<p>220b.1</p>pa'o// //dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rgyu'i rgyud kyi gang zag gi mtshan nyid can/ thabs kyi rgyud bskyed rdzogs gnyis te 'bras bu'i rgyud sku gsum ston pas/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba gsungs te/ gsang ba chos sku/ mchog longs sku/ yang mchog sprul sku/ 
<p>220b.2</p>de'i rig pa lha dang sngags phyag rgya chen po bshad pa ni mdor bstan to/ /rgyas bshad ni/ log pa'i shes pa'i lta ba la/ /cung zad ngas ni ma bstan gang / /zhes pa dor bya'i gang zag go/ /ji ltar bla ma'i rim pa bstan pa/ /zhes tshigs bcad phyed dang gnyis ni skye ba snga ma bsam
<p>220b.3</p>gtan dang zag med las skyes pa'i skal ldan blang bya ba'i gang zag go/ /lkugs shing glen la sdig ngan can/ /zhes bya ba tshigs bcad phyed dang gsum ni skal med dor bya'i gang zag bshad do/ /slob dpon bdag nyid chen po yis/ /zhes bya ba tshigs bcad gsum ni sngags
<p>220b.4</p>skyes kyi rnal 'byor pho mo thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes phab pas mthong ba reg pa thos pa dran pa las kyang sdig pa las grol bar the tshom med do/ /rgyu'i rgyud bshad nas/ thabs kyi rgyud bskyed rim thams cad kyi lha bzlog ste bkod pa sngags bzlog ste zlo ba ni g.yas skor dang
<p>220b.5</p>g.yon skor gyis ming bzlog pa zhes brtags te/ bskyed rim 'di ni rgyud sde bzhi thun mong du sems can yongs su ma smin pa las dang po pa la de bzhin gshegs pas dbugs dbyung ba gsungs pa/ bsod nams chung ba'i rnal 'byor pas kyang lha mnyes par byas pas dngos grub
<p>220b.6</p>bskyed par 'gyur ro/ /bskyed rim bshad nas zab pa'i rdzogs pa'i rim pa bde ba stong pa nyid bsgom pa la bsrung med bza' med ces bya ba nas mdor na sems ni mnyam nyid bya ba ni go sla'o/ /bla ma mnyes pa la brtson 'grus yod na rnam shes dga' ba bzhi dang ye shes sgyu ma 'od gsal
<p>220b.7</p>zung 'jug goms pas mngon gsum gyi lam ni tshig lung gis ma yin/ bstan bcos rjes dpag gis ma yin/ rnal 'byor pa'i rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i thabs kyi sems bde ba stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid dang rig pa bstan pa dang / dpa' bo rang yin par bstan pa dang bde stong mngon sum
<p>221a</p>
<p>221a.1</p>gyis grub na/ skad cig gi rnal 'byor phyag rgya lha kun dang gnas thams cad sngags kun skad cig ma gcig gis rtogs so/ /de ltar rdzogs pa'i rim pa bstan nas pus mo sa la gtsugs nas sgrub pa po lag na rdo rjes 'bras bu'i rgyud la gsol ba btab pa/ mya ngan
<p>221a.2</p>las 'das pa chos sku phyag rgya chen po longs spyod rdzogs pa'i ston pa gang nas gang du gnas par gyur nas brtan pa dang / g.yo ba sprul pa'i chos kyi rol pa bstan du gsol zhes pa dang / lan du legs par nyon la zhes skabs phye nas don dam par chos kyi sku las gzhan na med/ 
<p>221a.3</p>rnam rtog gi gzung 'dzin gyis bsam du med/ gzhan dbang gi gzung 'dzin dang bral ba'i sems kyi rang rig pa'i chos nyid la rtag tu da ltar byung ba bzhin du bzhugs so/ /de yang / thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs/ /zhes sngar bshad pa'i don ni rnal 'byor ba'i dkyil 'khor lus la brten
<p>221a.4</p>pa'i dbus nas gtum mo'i drod spar nas/ byang chub kyi sems phab pas rang rig pa'i stong nyid la nges pa drangs pa la thams cad mkhyen pa zhes bya/ rdo rje can de na bzhugs par byed pa 'dus ma byas dang / cha dang bcas pa 'dus byas spangs pa'i lus ni btsun mo'i b+ha ga zhes bya
<p>221a.5</p>bas lus kun la phung po lnga sangs rgyas/ dbang po drug sems dpa'/ 'byung ba rnams lha mor rol pa ste/ bde bar gshegs pas ji srid gsungs pa thams cad kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ mdor na phung po lnga dag ni/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas lnga ru grags/ /khams
<p>221a.6</p>dang skye mched mang po kun/ /byang chub sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor nyid/ /sa chu spyan dang mA ma kI/ /me rlung gos dkar sgrol ma ste/ /nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma/ /srid gsum ye nas sangs rgyas shing / /zhes bka' stsal to/ /rang rig pa'i stong nyid rtogs pa ni lus la
<p>221a.7</p>gnas kyang lus las ma skyes pa ste/ lus las dang nyon mongs pa'i snang bas ma bskyed pas na 'das zhes bya'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa byung yang rung ma byung yang rung ba'i zag pa med pa'i sa bon byang chub kyi snying po ni glo bur gyi dri mas gos pa med do/ /'o na mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba
<p>221b</p>
<p>221b.1</p>ji ltar snang zhe na/ mes du ba la phan 'dogs pa bzhin du rang rig pa don dang sems can du snang bas/ lus kun la ni rnam par grol/ /zhes bya'o/ /du bas me la phan mi 'dogs pa bzhin du dge mi dge zag bcas kyi lus las skyes pa ni chos sku dang longs sku bshad nas/ sprul pa'i sku ni snang bar 'chad
<p>221b.2</p>pa ni/ la lar gzugs can dag tu bshad/ /ces bya ba nas/ gang zhig thams cad bdag nyid bzhugs/ /zhes bya ba'i bar gyis zag pa med pa'i sa bon rang rig pa/ gnyis med 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid la bzhugs pa de ni sprul pa'i sku'i mtshan nyid lag
<p>221b.3</p>na rdo rje khyod la bstan pa yin no/ /gsang ba mchog gi dgyes pa ni sprul pa'i sku thams cad kyi bdag nyid bzhugs pa ni bshad zin to/ /chos kyi sku'i gsang ba mchog gi dgyes pa ni/ lha gang gi cha shas spangs pa sgyu ma sna tshogs pa 'di snang yang rtag tu bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes
<p>221b.4</p>b+ha ga chos nyid la bzhugs pa yin no/ /longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i gsang ba mchog gi dgyes pa na/ thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs pa ni lte ba'i dbus nas pad+ma 'dab ma bcu drug pa la yi ge dbugs 'byung rngub kyis dbugs bkag nas rtsa dang gnas pa'i rlung sbyar nas de'i
<p>221b.5</p>dbus na sems kyi stong pa nyid sprul pa'i sku 'byin zhes pa dang / sdud par byed pa nyid don dam pa'i de kho na nyid 'dus ma byas kyi ye shes rang byung bas 'dus byas kun la khyab pas chos sku'o/ /de ni sangs rgyas dngos zhes sprul pa'i skur mtshan brtags pa dang / rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i
<p>221b.6</p>mchog /ces kyang mtshan brtags pas thams cad mkhyen pa 'dus byas kyang kun du 'gro zhing 'dus byas kyi mi shigs pas rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog rgyud kyi gleng gzhi'i 'grel pa rnal 'byor pa'i rgyud la yod pa'i mdo sde 'dul ba mngon pa'i sku gsum dang mi mthun pa rjes su
<p>221b.7</p>mthun pa'i sku gsum 'bras bu'i rgyud bshad do/ /rdzogs rim thob pa'i rtags bshad pa ni/ skra'i rtse mo brgyar gshags pa'i cha'i tshad tsam ni a wa d+hU tI yin no/ /phra ba'i rdul ni byang chub kyi sems zla ba'i rgyun 'dzag pa yin no/ /stong pa nyid yang ma yin zhes pa ni rang rig pas
<p>222a</p>
<p>222a.1</p>myong ba'o/ /dmigs su med ces pa ni rtog pa dang bral ba'o/ /de ni dga' ba ste dbang po drug bde ba'o/ /yi ge med pa ni brjod bya rjod byed dang bral ba'o/ /stong pa ma yin zhes pa ni yul drug bde ba'o/ /rdul med ces pa ni tshogs drug gis 'dzin pa med pa'o/ /
<p>222a.2</p>srog med pa ni rlung dbus ma la brten pa'i rang rig par mngon par mi zhen pa lhan cig skyes dga'o/ /gzugs pa med ces bya ba ni mtshan gzhi lnga dang bral ba'o/ /mtshan ma med ces pa mtshan nyid gsum 'gags pa ste rnam pa thams cad kyi 'od gsal ba'o/ /rnam par shes pa'i
<p>222a.3</p>dngos po ni dga' ba gsum de'i ye shes ni sgyu ma 'od gsal zung 'jug go/ /ye shes skye ba'i rtags ni/ sgron ma lta bu dang po dang / mkha' snang lta bu gnyis pa dang / dkar po'i 'od zer 'phro ba gsum pa dang / 'dod pa'i lha'i longs spyod snang ba bzhi pa dang / gzugs kyi lha'i
<p>222a.4</p>bde bar snang ba lnga pa dang / gzugs med kyi ye shes bdun pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes brgyad pa dang / rgyud sde bzhi lha dgu ste 'dus ma byas kyi ye shes kyi rtags dgu skyes nas sa bcu'i dbang phyug thob pas khams gsum pa'i ye shes pa gzhan dag snying po med pa
<p>222a.5</p>rtswa dang mtshungs so/ /de ltar rgyu'i rgyud skal ldan dang skal med gnyis dang / thabs kyi rgyud bskyed rdzogs gnyis dang 'bras bu'i rgyud sku gsum dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i rtags drug bstan nas/ las dang po pas rdzogs pa'i rim pa ji ltar bsgom pa dang / bskyed pa'i rim pa ji
<p>222a.6</p>ltar bsgom pa bshad pa ni/ de kho na nyid don dam pa'i bden pa shes pa ni rgyu rkyen tshogs pa las te/ srog chags rnams kyi srog a wa d+hU tIr chud pa a na ha mi 'gyur ba zhes bya ba khyab byed kyi rlung de mtshungs pa de ma thag pa'i rkyen yin pas sems kyi 'dus ma byas shes pa de ni
<p>222a.7</p>sangs rgyas kyi ye shes dpal he ru kar bshad do/ /phyir rgyu ba skyes pa dang / nang du 'jug pa bud med dang / gnas pa bum pa'i rlung la ma ning zhes grags pa'o/ /de la sogs pa zhes pa ni dbugs nyi khri chig stong drug brgya bkag pa'i rlung dbus ma phra ba'i snying po 'dzin pa'i ye
<p>222b</p>
<p>222b.1</p>shes skye ba de la brten nas sa bcu dang / bstan bcos mngon shes drug dang rgyud sde bzhi rig byed kyi dngos grub dang / gang ji snyed gnas pa rnams srog a wa d+hU tIr chud pa 'di las byung ngo / /tshe 'di dang phyi mar yang rgyu rkyen tshogs pa med na dngos grub mi thob pas rgyud sde bzhi rig
<p>222b.2</p>byed grub mtha' la ye shes skye ba'i snying po gcig pu kho nas bshad do/ /yul dmigs pa'i rkyen 'dus ma byas tshogs ma bsags sgrib pa ma spangs kyang sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad las mthong bas rnyed sla/ gzhon nu ma'i lus dang yid bde ba bsam gtan gyi cha dbang po bdag po'i rkyen yang rnyed sla/ 
<p>222b.3</p>bag chags rgyu'i rkyen zag pa med pa'i sa bon byang chub kyi snying po yang rgyu yin pas rnyed sla'o/ /rkyen gsum po rnyed par sla yang / yid nang du chud pa rlung 'gags pa'i 'dod pa'i khams kyi sems can med pa ni rnyed par dka' bas man ngag gi gtso bo 'di yin no/ /de'i phyir/ ngo bo nyid kyi mthu dag
<p>222b.4</p>gis/ /rang bzhin gyis ni de 'grub bo/ /zhes rdzogs pa'i rim pa bshad nas/ bskyed pa'i rim pa thams cad kyi mdor bsdus pa'i yan lag bshad pa ni/ 'dug pa'am gnas pa ni sngon 'gro lnga'o/ /ldang ba ni 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rje pad+ma dang bdun no/ /'jug pa ni nyi zla kha
<p>222b.5</p>sbyor du sems 'jug pa'o/ /rdzogs pa ni sprul pa dang lus dang sems kyi 'khor lo/ byin rlabs ni go cha dang ye shes sems dpa' 'jug pa gnyis so/ /dbang bskur ba ni mchod pa dang bstod nas dbang bskur ba'o/ /ting nge 'dzin ni bsgom bzlas so/ /mchod pa ni bdud rtsi myang ba dang rkang pa
<p>222b.6</p>brgyad pa dang gtor ma gtong ba'o/ /nye bar bsdu ba ni dkyil 'khor lus la gzhug pa'o/ /spyir de ltar yin pa las skabs 'dir cho ga'i ming ni gzhan dag thabs shes rab kyi spro bsdu zhes bya ste/ dbyangs yig bcu drug ni shes rab bo/ /gsal byed sum cu rtsa bzhi ni thabs so/ /de gnyis
<p>222b.7</p>nyi zla kha sbyor gyi lha mo las lha thams cad bskyed par 'gyur ba'o/ /don dam pa dang kun rdzob ston pa'i chos kyi sgo mo brgyad khri bzhi stong yang yi ge phyi mo rnams las skyes/ sngags kyi spyod pa phrin las rnam bzhi thams cad kyi rgyud shes rab dang thabs A li kA li las 'gro zhing skye'o/ /thog
<p>223a</p>
<p>223a.1</p>ma'i dbyangs dang gsal byed ni zhi ba dang rgyas pa dge ba'i lha'am/ dbang dang mngon spyod mi dge ba'i lha'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor rgyan nam ska rags lta bu A li kA li las byung ngo / /de ltar las dang po pa'i bskyed pa'i rim pa rdzus skyes kyi sgrub pa'i thabs so/ /rdzogs
<p>223a.2</p>rim gyi dbang du byas nas A li kA li khrag dang byang chub sems kyi thig le la sogs te lte ba'i khrag gi thig le gtsub gtan/ dbus ma rtsa a wa d+hU tI srub shing / g.yas g.yon gyi rlung srub thag /bsrubs pa las khrag gi thig le las byung nas snying ga'i A li kA li byang chub kyi
<p>223a.3</p>sems bzhus pas gzhon nu ma'i bde ba lta bu ngal so/ /bde ba skyes pa la sems kyi chos nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus ma byas kyi sems myong bar mi rtag /sems de nyid don dam par bsams na 'dzin pa rdo rje 'chang thob par 'gyur ro/ /'di ni nang gi A li kA li don rang gi mtshan
<p>223a.4</p>nyid de rgyud sde bzhi gsang ba lag na rdo rje khyod la bshad pa yin no/ /bsod nams kyi tshogs lha'i 'khor lo dang / ye shes kyi tshogs 'dus ma byas rtogs pa gnyis ka'i rgyud bum pa so btang ba lta bu mi 'jigs pa thig le bsgom pa 'di 'bar bas spar bar bya'o/ /bskyed rim gyi dpa'
<p>223a.5</p>bo dang rnal 'byor ma thams cad kyang 'dis 'thob/ nges brjod bla ma'i rgyud kyi mngon sum gyi man ngag 'di snod min la mi bshad/ bshad na tshe 'dir sdug bsngal/ tshe phyi mar mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'bras bu mi 'thob bo/ /bum pa rlon pa lta bu ni bskyed rim lha'i 'khor lo yun ring por bsgoms
<p>223a.6</p>kyang rnam rtog gi snang bas 'jig pa dang / ye shes kyi tshogs dbu ma lta bu rjes dpag gi stong pa nyid bsgom pa yang bskal pa grangs med gcig gis sa dang po thob pas rnam rtog yun ring bas rdzogs par 'gyur la/ srog a wa d+hU tIr chud nas bde ba stong nyid bsgom pa ni 'dus ma byas
<p>223a.7</p>mngon sum gyis mthong ba'i lam bum pa so btang ba lta bu phyir mi ldog pa'i lam mi 'jig pa yin no/ /dper na bud med dang byis pa tshogs nas phan tshun kun du smra/ rjes su yi rang bas bsten yang don med pa de bzhin du bskyed rim dang rjes dpag gis lam dge ba zag bcas
<p>223b</p>
<p>223b.1</p>zag med ma bshad pas 'ching bar 'gyur ba yin no/ /mi'i lus po 'jim pa lta bu bskyed rim gyis bum pa lta bur bcos/ rjes dpag gis don dam pa'i lhar bcos kyang rung / dge ba zag bcas bum pa rlon pa dang 'dra/ srog a wa d+hU tIr chud nas bde ba stong pa mngon sum gyis grub pa'i tshe rnal 'byor
<p>223b.2</p>lus brtan pa gzugs dang / g.yo ba tshor ba 'du shes 'du byed rnam par shes pa kun dpal he ru ka'i sku'i yan lag bcu gnas bcur mkha' 'gro ma'i brda ming btags pa/ mtho ris thugs dang sa stengs gsung dang sa 'og sku'i dpa' bo'i yan lag brtan g.yo thams cad he ru ka'i phyag
<p>223b.3</p>dang zhabs dang mig spyan du 'gyur/ mgo bo dbur 'gyur/ byang zhal du 'gyur/ rna ba snyan du 'gyur/ 'jig rten na yod pa thams cad g.yogs pa bzhin du mngon sum du grub nas brjod byar bzhugs so/ /A li kA li bum pa so btang ba lta bu'i thig le'i 'khor lo bde mchog bstan pa yin
<p>223b.4</p>no/ /da ni mngal skyes kyi 'bras bu dang bcas pa bshad pa ni/ de nas dngos grub bsgrub bya ba/ /zhes bya ba gsungs te/ mngal skyes kyi bsam gtan gyi sems don bcu bzhis sa bcas pa sgrub pa po la phan pa'i phyir gsungs so/ /de nas gzhan yang mdo sde dang rgyud dag tu sbas pa'i dpa'
<p>223b.5</p>bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i brda ni dang po'o/ /gos stod g.yogs dang smad g.yogs dang phyag mtshan lnga cod pan dang rgyan la sogs pa ni lus kyi kun du spyod pa gnyis pa'o/ /shes rab mdun du gzhag pa ni gsum mo/ /phur bu dang dra ba la sogs pa ni srung ba'i 'khor bzhi pa'o/ /A li
<p>223b.6</p>kA li brjod pa bsod nams kyi tshogs sogs pa lnga pa'o/ /rnam thar sgo gsum gyi rgyud la sogs pa stong pa ye shes kyi tshogs ni drug pa'o/ /nyi zla kha sbyor du sems 'jug pa'i yig 'bru dang phyag mtshan la sogs pas lhar bskyed pa ni bdun pa'o/ /rgyu'i he ru ka gsungs pa ni
<p>223b.7</p>brgyad pa'o/ /glu'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni dgu pa'o/ /bdud rtsi tshim byed myang ba dang ye shes sems dpa' bcu pa'o/ /lag pa'i mchod pas go cha bskon pa ni bcu gcig pa'o/ /dbang bskur ba ni bcu gnyis pa'o/ /go cha chen po lus kyi dkyil 'khor dang sems kyi dkyil
<p>224a</p>
<p>224a.1</p>'khor bsgom pa ni bcu gsum pa'o/ /sngags kyi mchod bstod gtor ma gtang ba ni bcu bzhi pa'o/ /mi mchog gang zhig kun spyod pa/ /zhes bya ba tshigs bcad phyed dang gnyis ni smon lam dang yon no/ /'bras bu ni zla ba nya la mtshan ma thob nas dngos grub blangs nas
<p>224a.2</p>zag med kyi ye shes dang ldan pas mtho ris kyi longs spyod lha'i 'khor los sgyur ba dngos grub 'bring / mi'i 'khor los sgyur ba dngos grub tha ma/ rnal 'byor pa 'pho ba'i tshe mkha' spyod kyi gnas bde ba can nam/ mngon par dga' bar khrid nas skyes pa ni dngos grub rab bo/ /le'u lnga
<p>224a.3</p>bcu rtsa drug gi 'grel pa'o// //dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sngags btu ba/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba smos te rgyud 'dir btu ba'i thabs kyang bzhi/ 'bras bu bcu gcig yin no/ /de la rtsa ba'i rgyud las e gru gsum gyi dbus su pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad la sde tshan brgyad
<p>224a.4</p>bkod pa ni btu ba'i gnas dang po'o/ /rdo rje mkha' 'gro las gzhal yas khang gi dbus su re'u mig bzhi bcu rtsa dgu gris pa ni btu ba'i gnas gnyis pa'o/ /rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u sum cu rtsa gcig pa nas rdza rnga'i dbyibs kyi nang du re'u mig bzhi bcu rtsa dgu byas nas btu ba'i gnas gsum
<p>224a.5</p>pa'o/ /mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud phyi ma las pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad dang mtshams bzhi dang bcas pa las byung ba ni bzhi pa'o/ /btu ba'i thabs ni bzhi ste dbyangs dang gsal byed kyis btu ba dang / ming gis btu ba dang / lha'i 'khrul 'khor gyis btu ba dang / phyed btus pa ste bzhi'o/ /'bras
<p>224a.6</p>bu ni bcu gcig ste yab yum gyi snying po bzhi dang / dpa' bo dang dpa' mo'i sngags gnyis dang go cha gnyis dang rkang pa brgyad pa'i sngags gnyis dang / gnod mdzes kyi sngags dang bcu gcig go/ /'dir sngags btu ba ni dben pa'i gnas su bdud rtsi lngas byugs la/ bdag nyid
<p>224a.7</p>he ru kar bskyed nas dmangs rigs kyi khrag gis thig le dang me tog dgod pa dang bdug pa dang mar me dang cang te'u dang glu gar gyis mchod nas phyag rgya drug dang ldan pa'i lus kyis srung ba'i 'khor lo byas te/ e gru gsum gyi dbus su/ A li kA li sde tshan brgyad bsdebs
<p>224b</p>
<p>224b.1</p>pas bzhi bzhi brgyad du byas nas dang por rtsa ba'i sngags kyi gsal byed btu ba ni go sla'o/ /rkang pa brgyad pa dang / ka ra ka ra la sogs pa rtsa ba'i sngags btu ba yin no/ /de'i phan yon ni rig pa rgyal ba'i gsang sngags te bya ba dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa zag bcas kyi 'jig rten gsum na
<p>224b.2</p>dpal he ru ka zag med kyi sngags shes na mchog yin no/ /le'u lnga bcu rtsa bdun pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang yab kyi snying po yi ge nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa lha dang sbyar nas 'khrul 'khor gyis btus/ nye ba'i snying po yang lha dang sbyar nas btus zin/ ya tshogs brgyad pa ha la
<p>224b.3</p>dbyangs bcu gnyis dang sbyar ba ha ring po la sogs pa drug phyi la dor bar bya'o/ /ha thung ngu drug dang oM na ma swA hA bau Sha Ta hUM hUM phaT kyi sngags dang sbyar bas gnas drug tu go cha drug tu 'gyur ba ni go sla'o/ /de nas dbyangs yig bcu gsum pa ni o/ yi ge gnyis pa ni ma dag dang sbyor ba ni mor
<p>224b.4</p>'gyur ro/ /dbyangs yig bcu gnyis pa ni e/ yi ge drug pa ni ha/ brgyad pa ni her 'gyur ro/ /dbyangs kyi zhi ba ni I/ yi ge bdun pa ni ba/ sbyar ba ni bIr 'gyur ro/ /dbyangs yig bcu gnyis pa ni ai yi ge brgyad pa nir/ mkhas pas sbyar ba ni rer 'gyur ro/ /dbyangs yig gnyis pa ni A/ 
<p>224b.5</p>yi ge dgu pa ni sha/ brgyad pas ni shA ring por 'gyur ro/ /de ltar na na mo b+ha ga wa te bI re shA ya'i sngags su 'gyur ro/ /lhag ma ni go sla'o/ /yab kyi snying po dang nye ba'i snying po go bzlog nas bris pa ni mngon spyod dbang las zlos pa'o/ /yum gyi snying po dang go cha'i lha mo drug gi ming dang po dang
<p>224b.6</p>bsdebs pas sngags drug tu 'gyur ro/ /go cha'i sngags gnyis ni phyed btus pa'o/ /le'u lnga bcu rtsa brgyad pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang lha mo'i snying po yi ge bcu gsum pa lha bskyed pa'i sa bon 'khrul 'khor gyi sngags btu ba ni/ snying po bla med bshad par bya/ /zhes
<p>224b.7</p>pa'o/ /sngon 'gro lnga dang / 'byung ba bzhi dang ri rab sna tshogs rdo rje gzhal yas khang dang drug bskyed nas/ de'i dbus su drod gsher skyes kyi yum gyi snying po dang sbyor ba'o/ /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho ni pad+ma'i dbus su phag mo ha las bskyed pa dang / 'dab ma brgyad pa gsal byed la oM las
<p>225a</p>
<p>225a.1</p>ba las rta gdong ma/ dzra las rdo rje ma/ bai las dpa' mo/ ro las khyo byed ma/ rtsa las gsod ma/ nI las khug rna ma/ ye las zung ldan ma dang brgyad do/ /hUM las shar sgor hUM mdzad ma/ hUM rings las lho skor sreg mdzad ma/ phaT las nub sgor phaT mdzad ma/ swA las byang sgor zhi
<p>225a.2</p>mdzad ma/ drod gsher skyes kyi 'khor los yum gyi snying po yang btus so/ /sku mdog dang phyag mtshan rgyud na gsal/ ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / go cha bgo ba dang / dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myang ba dang / bsgom pa dang / lha mo bcu gnyis kyi spyi'i snying po bzlas pa dang / 
<p>225a.3</p>mchod pa dang / gtor ma btang bas kha bskang ngo / /le'u lnga bcu rtsa dgu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas gzhan yang gnod mdzes kyi sngags btu ba bshad pa ni/ rdo rje rol pa rta'i 'gros dang / yi dwags srin po'i gdong dang / gshin rje dbyig pa 'chang ba dang / ma mo rigs kyi 'khor
<p>225a.4</p>lo gnod mdzes kyi sngags las byung bas shin tu rnyed par dka' ba ste/ 'khrul 'khor de rnams gang zhig gis shes pa tsam gyis myur du dngos grub thob bo/ /mdor bstan nas rgyas par bshad pa ni/ sa'i cha mnyam pa la tsan+dan gyis byugs nas me tog dang spos kyis mchod la/ bdag nyid
<p>225a.5</p>shes rab kyi yan lag dang bcas pas phyogs bcings la/ rdza rnga kha bzhi pa bri ste/ re'u mig bzhi bcu rtsa dgu pa la yi ge'i phyi mo bkod pa gnas de las dpa' bo sum+b+ha ni btu'o/ /rim gyis btu ba'am rim las bzlog nas btu ba ni go sla'o/ /de nyid bsdus pa dang / dpal mchog
<p>225a.6</p>dang / bde mchog mnyam sbyor dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed la sogs par shar sngo ba/ lho ser ba/ nub dmar ba/ byang ljang ba'i khro bo bzhi dang / mtshams su phyed gzugs kyi khro bo brgyad dang bcas pa dkyil 'khor bsrung ba'i don du steng 'og gi gdug pa kun 'dul ba'i khro bo bcu
<p>225a.7</p>bsgom pa'am/ yang na khro bo bzhi bsgom par bya'o/ /sha chen la sogs pa bdud rtsi lnga'i ri lus le'u bzhi pa las bshad pa bzhin du nang gi sbyin sreg byas nas rdo rje can brgya byin yang 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /sngags ni go sla'o/ /dkyil 'khor ni nam mkha'i khams su pad+ma 'dab
<p>225b</p>
<p>225b.1</p>brgyad kyi lte ba'i dbus su yi ge hUM las hUM mdzad zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug par bsgom pa ni rgyud na gsal lo/ khro bo bzhi ni shar du 'dod pa'i rdo rje sngo ba/ byang du rdo rje rnon po ljang ba/ nub tu stobs rdo rje dmar ba/ lho ru mi g.yo rdo rje ser nag /bdud bzhi gnon pa/ shar 'khor lo dang
<p>225b.2</p>dril bu/ lhor rin po che dang dril bu/ nub tu pad+ma dang dril bu/ byang du rgya gram dang dril bu/ rang gi mtshan ma dril bur bcas/ /zhes pa thams cad kyang khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba'i phyag rgya bcings pa zhal gsum phyag drug pa bsgoms la ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa
<p>225b.3</p>dang go cha bskon pa dang dbang bskur ba dang / dpral ba lkog ma snying gar sku gsung thugs kyi sbyor ba bsgom/ sum cu rtsa bdun gyi rnam dag yang bsgom/ sum+b+ha na'i sngags bzlas/ ma grub na bskyar ba'i cho ga nang gi sbyin sreg khyi'i gzugs kyi ling+gas zhe sdang bza' ba dang / phag gi
<p>225b.4</p>ling+gas gti mug bza' ba dang / khyim bya'i ling+gas 'dod chags bza' ba dang / mkha' 'gro la yang gtor ma bya ba dang / dung dang nya phyis dang mu tig rnams srog chags kyi rgyu las byung ba khyad par med kyang mi'i thod pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi rgyud las byung bas/ dpa'
<p>225b.5</p>bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i rgyan byas pa la smad par mi bya'o/ /tshogs kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i cho ga'o/ /le'u drug cu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi 'gro ba 'dul ba grong khyer dgug pa'i sngags kyi dkyil 'khor bshad pa ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba
<p>225b.6</p>smos te slob dpon Ar+ya de bas shar phyogs dri za'i yul du phyin nas 'gro ba mi dad pa las sde tshan brgyad kyi yi ge'i lha bkod nas sngags drag po bzlas pas rgyal po dang bcas pa g.yo ba dang / sems dga' bas btul ba bzhin du/ sde tshan brgyad kyis bsgom pa 'byung ba bzhi dang ri rab
<p>225b.7</p>bzhi 'gyur ba'i nam mkha'i dbyings kyi gzhal yas khang gi pad+ma'i dbus su hUM las rdo rje he ru ka drod gsher skyes zhal lnga phyag bcu gnyis yum baM las byung ba dang 'khyud pa 'jigs byed chung ma dang bcas pa zhabs kyi 'og tu mnan pa/ sku mdog dang phyag mtshan ni go sla'o/ /shar gyi 'dab
<p>226a</p>
<p>226a.1</p>ma la a las mkha' 'gro ma dkar mo/ byang du pa las mkha' 'gro ma dmar mo/ nub tu tsa las mkha' 'gro ma ser mo/ lhor ka las mkha' 'gro ma sngon mo/ shar lhor Ta las mkha' 'gro ma dmar mo/ lho nub tu ta las mkha' 'gro ma dud ka /nub byang du ya las mkha' 'gro
<p>226a.2</p>ma ljang gu/ byang shar du sha las mkha' 'gro ma ser mo zhal gcig phyag bzhi ma/ 'jig rten skyong ba brgyad mnan pa/ sku mdog dang phyag mtshan ni go sla'o/ /yul de'i bud med rgyal mo byed na rdo rje phag mo dbus su gzhag /ye shes sems dpa' gzhug /go cha bskon/ dbang bskur/ bdud
<p>226a.3</p>rtsi myang / sku gsung thugs kyi 'khor lo nang du bsgom/ de nas rang thag gis phye 'thag pa ltar bsgoms la/ oM a ka tsa Ta ta pa ya sha hUM phaT swA hA zhes bya ba zlos shing nam mkha' stong pa e gru gsum pa'i b+ha ga'i dbus su yul gyi ming rgyal po dang bcas pa gzhag /rang gi dkyil 'khor
<p>226a.4</p>dang bsre/ de nas 'khor lo bskor ro/ /ma grub na tshogs kyi 'khor lo byas la rta dang wa dang pha wang la sogs pa'i sha yi ge brgyad kyi dang por byas pa'i 'bras bu btags pa'i phye ma'i gzugs brnyan byas nas tshogs kyi 'khor lo byas na mngon par shes pa skye/ skye ba bdun pa'i mtshan nyid
<p>226a.5</p>kyang shes nas de'i sha zos na myur du mkha' la 'gro bar the tshom med do/ /le'u drug cu rtsa gcig pa'i 'grel pa'o// //dkyil 'khor thams cad bsgoms pa las mtshan ma thob na mngon shes bskyed par bya ba'i dkyil 'khor ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /
<p>226a.6</p>zhes bya ba'o/ /mtshan ma thob nas rang dad pa'i dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma gcig la gsol ba btab nas 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnal 'byor ba nyi shu rtsa lnga dang rnal 'byor ma sum cu rtsa bdun ye shes las skyes pa'am/ zhing skyes khug la spyon zhes bcol la tshogs kyi 'khor lo bya ba'am
<p>226a.7</p>yang na rang gis dbang bskur ba'i rnal 'byor ba dang / rnal 'byor ma srog a wa d+hU tIr chud pa sngags skyes su byas la/ gdong rgyan ye shes kyi 'khor lo'i lha lnga bong bu'i gdong rgyan bskon/ yum rdo rje phag mo phag gi gdong rgyan bskon/ sngar bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor gang la mos pa zhal
<p>226b</p>
<p>226b.1</p>gcig phyag gnyis pa'am/ zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa'am zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sku mdog dang phyag mtshan sngar bshad pa'i rim pa bzhin du/ thugs kyi kun nam mkha' lding gi gdong can/ gsung gi kun rma bya'i gdong can/ sku'i 'khor lo brgyad kyi lha seng ge'i gdong can/ sgo bzhir khwa
<p>226b.2</p>gdong la sogs pa'i gdong can/ mtshams bzhir ma he'am ri dwags kyi gdong can gyi dkyil 'khor spyan nyi ma dang zla ba dang me'i mig gsum 'bar bar bsgoms la mngon shes drug bskyed do/ /blo ldan rig 'dzin gyi rnal 'byor ba 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba shes pa'i dngos grub dang / rnal
<p>226b.3</p>'byor pa la mchog ster ba zag pa zad pa'i mngon shes dang / rdo rje theg pa'i man ngag skye ba dran pa dang / mngon shes dang ngag gi dngos grub rgyud sde bzhi 'chad shes pa lha'i rna ba shes pa dang / ma thos pa'i chos bstan pas sems can grol ba gzhan gyi sems shes pa dang / mi snang ba
<p>226b.4</p>la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi yul shes pa dang / 'jig rten gsum skad cig gis mthong ba thob bo/ /mngon shes drug thob nas dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i sngags bzlas pa'i dngos grub gang 'dod pa rtag tu bde blag tu thob par 'gyur ro/ /mngon shes ma skyes na nye ba'i snying po rnal 'byor
<p>226b.5</p>pas bzlas nas pra se na bya sna bong bu'i rnam pa'i mngon shes 'thob bo/ /mngon shes thob nas dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma sngags bzlas pa'i dngos grub gang 'dod pa ma grub na bskyar ba'i cho ga gdong brnyan gon nas lo gcig gam zla ba drug gam zla ba gsum mam/ khwa la sogs pa
<p>226b.6</p>srog chags brgyad kyi sha dang / bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga bza' zhing bsam gtan gyi bsgom bzlas byas na myur du dngos grub thob bo/ /rdzu 'phrul gyi yul shes pa tshangs pa dang khyab 'jug gi chung ma'am/ lha dang mi'i bu mo gang dang gnas pa bza' ba bdud rtsi lngar byin gyis ma brlabs
<p>226b.7</p>pa dang bgrod pas dbang bskur ba dang / bgrod min dbang ma bskur ba dang / btung ba bdud rtsi'i chu dang / bdud rtsi ma yin pas kyang 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /mkha' 'gro ma lA ma'i gzugs dang / bu mo dang sring mo la sogs pa'i gzugs kyi rnal 'byor pa ci 'dod pa'i phyag rgya
<p>227a</p>
<p>227a.1</p>chen po srog a wa d+hU tIr chud nas stong pa nyid rtogs pas 'grub pa'o/ /rdo rje gdan bzhi las b+ha ba na mu kha zhes bya ba lte bar rlung zhugs nas stong nyid bsgom pa la ming 'dogs te/ bong bu'i mkha' 'gro bsgoms nas ni/ /bkug na myur du dngos grub 'gyur/ /
<p>227a.2</p>zhes bshad do/ /le'u drug cu rtsa gnyis pa'i 'grel pa'o// //de nas dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i 'khor lo ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba ni rigs lnga'i 'khor lo rang rang gi gnas su so so'i sa bon dang phyag mtshan las skyes pa'i 'khor lo ste mdor
<p>227a.3</p>bstan pa'o/ /rgyas par bshad pa ni sa bon gyi mchog nga nya Na na ma lnga las gtso bo bskyed pa ni sngon 'gro lnga byas nas 'byung ba bzhi ri rab dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang gzhal yas khang bskyed pa dang / gdan dang sku mdog dang gtso bo dang 'khor lha'i ming dang phyag mtshan dang / sgo ba rnams kyi
<p>227a.4</p>ming dang sku mdog dang phyag mtshan dang / phyi rol du yi dwags kyis yongs su bskor ba bsgom par bya zhes pa dkyil 'khor rgyal mchog go sla'o/ /las kyi rgyal mchog ni thog mar oM dang bar du ming dang mthar hUM phaT dang bcas pas bzlas par bya/ de'i sngon du go cha bskon ye shes
<p>227a.5</p>sems dpa' gzhug /phung po dang khams dang skye mched byin gyis brlab/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro gal te mos nas zhal drug phyag bcu gnyis pa dbus ma sngo ba/ g.yas ser ba/ rgyab dmar ba/ g.yon ljang gu/ lnga pa dud ka ste steng ma'o/ /de'i steng ma zhi ba dkar po'o/ /shar phyogs
<p>227a.6</p>kyi sangs rgyas mkha' 'gro dbus dkar/ g.yas sngo/ /rgyab ser ba/ g.yon dmar ba/ lnga pa ste ljang gu/ drug pa thal ba'i mdog can/ lho'i rin chen mkha' 'gro dbus ser ba/ g.yas sngo/ rgyab dkar/ g.yon dmar/ lnga pa ljang gu ste steng ma drug pa dmar ba'o/ /nub phyogs pad+ma'i
<p>227a.7</p>mkha' 'gro dbus dmar ba/ g.yas dkar ba/ rgyab sngo ba/ g.yon ser ba/ steng lnga pa ljang gu/ drug pa nam mkha'i mdog can no/ /byang phyogs su las kyi mkha' 'gro dbus ljang / g.yas dkar/ rgyab dmar/ g.yon sngo steng ma/ lnga pa ser ba/ drug pa dkar po'o/ /phyag dang po dbus
<p>227b</p>
<p>227b.1</p>rdo rje dang dril bu/ shar 'khor lo dang dril bu/ lho rin po che dang dril bu/ nub pad+ma dang dril bu/ byang rgya gram dang dril bu/ thams cad kyi g.yas g.yon gnyis pa gnyis na mdung rtse gsum pa dang lcags kyu/ gsum pa gnyis na thod pa dang kha T+wAM ga/ /bzhi pa gnyis na mgo bo dang cang
<p>227b.2</p>te'u/ lnga pa gnyis na mdung dang gri gug /drug pa gnyis kyis mi lpags 'dzin pa'o/ /'khor rnams zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa phyag mtshan dang sku mdog ni rgyud na gsal lo/ /yang na gtso 'khor thams cad zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ de la ye shes sems dpa'i gzhug /go
<p>227b.3</p>cha bskon/ dbang bskur/ bdud rtsi myang / bsgom pa bya bzlas pa bya/ mchod pa dang bstod pa byas la dkyil 'khor thams cad du dbang bskur ba ni 'dir dbang bskur thams cad kyi gsang ba dang shes rab ye shes su 'gyur ro/ /dbang bskur ba dngos bshad pa ni/ sna tshogs pa ni du
<p>227b.4</p>mar dga'/ /zhes bya ba sna tshogs ni dus su/ du mar dga' ba ni dbang po drug gi dga' ba'o/ /rtags ni 'khyud pa dang tsum pa ka'o/ /rnam smin ni dus su ye shes dam pa ni mchog dga' yul drug bde ba'o/ /b+ha gar ling+ga sbyor ba ni rtags so/ /rnam par 'joms pa ni dus so/ /phyag rgya bskyod pa ni dus
<p>227b.5</p>so/ /shin tu dga' ba ni mtshan nyid do/ /mtshan nyid dang bral ba ni dus so/ /rang rig pa'i tshad mas nges par brtags pa ni rtags so/ /lhan cig skyes dga' ni mtshan nyid do/ /de ltar dga' ba dbang po drug bde ba dang / mchog dga' yul drug bde
<p>227b.6</p>ba dang / shin tu dga' ba rnam par shes pa drug bde bar rang rig pa sgro 'dogs dang bral ba lhan cig skyes dga' 'dus ma byas la dmigs pas bla na med pa'o/ /rnal 'byor dang rjes su rnal 'byor dang / shin tu rnal 'byor dang rnal 'byor chen po'i ye shes kyi cho ga'i rim pa'o/ /
<p>227b.7</p>de ltar dga' ba bzhi bum pa dang gsang ba dang shes rab ye shes dang dbang bzhi pa'i don thig le'i rnal 'byor shes pa las kyang ste/ phra mo'i rnal 'byor las kyang thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi nye bar len pa'i rgyud sems kyis chos kyi dbyings rtogs na myur du 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /
<p>228a</p>
<p>228a.1</p>de ltar rab gnas kyi le'u nas brtsams nas dbang bskur ba'i le'u'i bar du le'u bcu drug pa/ dang po sku'i 'khor lo bsgom pa nas le'u drug cu rtsa brgyad pa so sor 'brang ma'i bar gyi rab gnas dang / dbang bskur dang bstod pa dang snying po nye snying dang / rnam dag dang rgyud kyi don
<p>228a.2</p>dang tshogs 'khor dang sngags btu ba dang dngos grub len pa dang srung 'khor dang nang gi dbang bzhi len pa ni le'u thams cad kyi yan lag tu 'gyur ro/ /le'u drug cu rtsa gsum pa'i 'grel pa'o// //da ni dbang du bya ba lha mo bzhi zhus dang / mngon spyod rdo rje 'jigs byed dang / zhi ba sgyu
<p>228a.3</p>'phrul dra ba dang / rgyas pa so sor 'brang ma dang / bskyar ba'i cho ga skye ba bdun pa'i sha ste lnga bshad pa yin no/ /nang gi sems dang / phyi rol gyi 'gro ba rigs drug dbang du bya ba ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba gsungs so/ /sngon 'gro lnga dang 'byung ba bzhi
<p>228a.4</p>ri rab sna tshogs rdo rjer gyur pa las/ nam mkha'i dbus su gzhal yas khang bsgoms te/ rdo rje sems dpa' thugs kyi snying po nyi zla kha sbyor gyi dbus su yi ge a las rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba chen po kha ba kun+da shel gyi mdog lta bu zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' rnam
<p>228a.5</p>par bsgom zhes bya ba'i bar du go sla'o/ /I las rdo rje zla ba ma sangs rgyas spyan/ i las rdo rje sgyu 'phrul mA ma kI / e las chos kyi rdo rje ma gos dkar mo/ /ai las sna tshogs rdo rje sgyu 'phrul ma sgrol ma ste thams cad zhal gsum phyag drug pa kun kyang dkar ba/ g.yas sngo ba/ g.yon
<p>228a.6</p>dmar ba/ rdo rje dang dril bu gnyis/ mdung dang gri gug gnyis thod pa dang kha T+wAM ga gnyis/ phyag mtshan drug 'dzin pa'o/ /gtso bo bskyed pa bsnyen pa/ 'khor bskyed pa nye bar bsnyen pa/ lha mo bzhi'i dbus su gsang ba'i sgron ma chos kyi dbyings kyi yum dang 'khyud pa 'khor gyi lha mo bzhi yang
<p>228a.7</p>rang snang ba'i thabs dang kha sbyor ba'o/ /sgrub pa ni snying gar u las rdo rje sems dpa' mgo bor o thung las rnam snang / spyi gtsug tu au ring po las pad+ma gar gyi dbang phyug/ mig tu U ring gnyis las rdo rje nyi ma/ phrag pa gnyis su aM las he ru ka /yan lag lnga la a las rta mchog /lus
<p>228b</p>
<p>228b.1</p>kyi nang du sku gsung thugs kyi 'khor lo gsum dang / phyi rol gyi lus la 'khor lo gsum gyi lha bkod la bsgom pa ni sgrub pa'o/ /sgrub pa chen po ye shes sems dpa' spyan drangs la mchod pa dang gnyis su med par ro gcig par bsgom pa dang / bdud rtsi myangs pa'i rjes la nang par sangs rgyas spyan dang / kha sbyar
<p>228b.2</p>gyi dga' ba bzhi bsgom/ nyi phyed la mA ma kI dang kha sbyar ba dga' ba bzhi bsgom/ srod la gos dkar mo dang kha sbyar ba'i dga' ba bzhi bsgom/ mtshan phyed na sgrol ma dang kha sbyar ba'i dga' ba bzhi bsgom/ skya rengs shar khar stong nyid kyis rgyas btab nas cha med 'dus ma byas bsgom/ 
<p>228b.3</p>cha bcas sgyu ma lta bu rdo rje sems dpa' cha med 'dus ma byas 'od gsal ba rdzogs rim bsgoms la/ bskyed rim bsgom pa ni/ ye shes kyi bzlas pa dpral bar sku'i 'khor lo/ /lkog mar gsung gi 'khor lo/ snying gar thugs kyi 'khor lo/ /nu ma'i bar du ye shes kyi 'khor lo/ 
<p>228b.4</p>lte bar dam tshig gi 'khor lo/ phyi rol gyi lus kyi dkyil 'khor dang drug gi spro bsdu bsgom sngags go sla'o/ /rdzogs pa'i rim pa bsgom pa ni/ sdig pa dag par byed/ bsod nams che/ dge bas zag bcas kyi nyes pa 'joms/ sdug bsngal 'joms/ bde ba ster/ sngags kun
<p>228b.5</p>ston sangs rgyas bskyed/ mkha' 'gro ma kun 'byung shin tu dag pa'i sa bcu'i sems dpa' 'byung / de'i thabs lha mo bzhi las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / mchog dga' bde ba rigs kyi dga' ba lhan cig skyes dga' rang 'byung bde ba chen po rdo rje sems dpa' yin no/ /le'u drug cu rtsa bzhi
<p>228b.6</p>pa'i 'grel pa'o// //mngon spyod kyi rdo rje 'jigs byed bsgom pa ni/ de nas rnal 'byor mchog bshad pa/ /zhes bya ba gsungs te/ las dang nyon mongs pa'i gdug pa zad par byed pa dang phyi'i bgegs stong phrag brgyad cu nang gi nad bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i sdug bsngal 'joms pa la dgos pa'o/ /
<p>228b.7</p>sngon 'gro lnga dang 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rjer gyur pa las stong pa nam mkha'i dbus su gzhal yas khang de'i dbus su yi ge k+Sha yongs su gyur pa las rdo rje 'jigs byed zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa bsgom pa ni go sla'o/ /gang zag sus bsgom zhe na/ stong pa nyid kyi blo can
<p>229a</p>
<p>229a.1</p>'jigs pa spangs pa rnam par rtog pa bcom pa tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'du 'dzi spangs pa'i rten gyi gang zag gis bsgom mo/ /gnas gang du bsgom zhe na/ shin tu bgrod dka'i dur khrod ces pa go sla'o/ /yang na zhal bzhi phyag brgyad pa'i zhal dbus ma sngo ba/ g.yas dkar ba
<p>229a.2</p>g.yon dmar ba/ steng ser ba/ phyag dang po rdo rje dang dril bu/ rdo rje dang thod pa mdung dang cang te'u/ mgo bo dang gri gug thogs pa'o/ yang na ma he'i gdong can zhal dgu phyag sum cu rtsa bzhi pa bsgom mo/ /ma he'i gdong can ni phyag sum cu rtsa bzhis sna tshogs pa'i mtshon cha bsnams
<p>229a.3</p>pa ma he'i zhal gyi ljags bskyod pa/ zhal lhag ma brgyad kyis ha ha hi hi hUM hUM phaT phaT brgyad sgrogs pa dang / dpa' bo gcig pu 'od zer 'phros pas 'jigs par mdzad pa phyogs skyong ba brgyad dang chung ma mkha' 'gro ma brgyad gdul dka' thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ye shes
<p>229a.4</p>sems dpa' bcug go cha bskon dbang bskur sgom pa'i tshe sku gsung thugs kyi khro bo spro dam tshig gi spro bsdu byas nas bzlas/ phan yon ni khams gsum gyi sdig pa za ba dang / mtshams med pa lnga byed pa za ba dang / sdug bsngal srid pa sbyong / bklags pas 'grub pa yin no/ /las la
<p>229a.5</p>sbyor ba'i tshe na gdug pa can dang gnod pa can gyi ling+ga byas la/ sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa pho nya spros nas ma rungs pa bkug nas/ ming dang bcas pa'i sngags bzla zhing sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga za zhing gcer bu skra grol ba lus kyi spyod pa lcags kyu dang zhags pa lag pas bzung nas sngags khri
<p>229a.6</p>phrag stong bzlas na khams gsum po yang gsod par 'gyur ro/ /yang na mkha' 'gro ma sum cu rtsa drug 'khor gyis bskor bar bsams la thams cad kyang rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i khro bo dgra bo'i snying du zhugs nas snying dang rgyu ma la sogs pa drangs nas za bar byed par bsams nas zhag
<p>229a.7</p>bdun gyi nyi ma phyed dang mtshan phyed na kha lhor bltas nas tsher ma can gyi me la hUM phaT raM raM zhes bya ba'i sngags zlos shing / mar ngo'i bcu bzhi la sbyin sreg byas na rdo rje 'dzin pa brgya byin yang 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /rang la 'bangs byas skyabs su song na 'o ma can gyi shing la zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bya ba ni
<p>229b</p>
<p>229b.1</p>go sla'o/ /le'u drug cu rtsa lnga pa'i 'grel pa'o// //gal te tshe 'di la bsnyen pa byas kyang ma grub na rten 'brel gyi mthu skye ba bdun pa'i shas 'grub par 'gyur te/ de nas yang dag bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba smos so/ /skye ba bdun pa'i mtshan nyid ni/ lha'i gzugs can ni rtags
<p>229b.2</p>dang po'o/ /snyan par smra ba gnyis pa/ gsum pa bde bar gshegs la dga' ba/ bzhi pa skra ring pa/ lnga pa mig dkyus ring ba/ drug pa mig pad+ma lta bu/ bdun pa rdul dri zhim pa dang / brgyad pa glang po'i dri yod pa/ dgu pa ga bur gyi dri yod pa/ bcu pa bshang gci gla rtsi'i dri yod pa/ 
<p>229b.3</p>bcu gcig pa tshig 'jam pa/ bcu gnyis pa lag pa rkang pa 'jam pa/ bcu gsum pa ut+pala'i dri yod pa/ bcu bzhi pa skra dkar dang gnyer ma med pa/ bco lnga pa lus mdangs dang ldan pa/ bcu drug pa snying dang klad pa ni gi'u wang yod pa/ bcu bdun pa grib ma bdun yod pa/ bco brgyad
<p>229b.4</p>pa ngang pa'i 'gros su 'gro ba/ bcu dgu pa snying rje can/ nyi shu pa dkon mchog gsum la dad pa/ rtags nyi shu rtsa gcig pa pha rol du phyin pa drug dang ldan pa de lta bu rnal 'byor pas rtogs na/ de la phyi rtags dus ma yin par 'chi ba brgyad kyis mi tshugs seng ge dang stag dang spyang kis
<p>229b.5</p>mi za des mtshan mo mthong la nyin mo mi snang / de lta bu rtogs nas khyod grongs na bdag la khyed kyi lus sbyin par mdzad du gsol zhes blang bar bya'o/ /de nas rnal 'byor pas bdud rtsi lnga lcags gsum gyis dkris pa khar bcug nas yab yum gyi snying po lhar bskyed dbang po sbyangs
<p>229b.6</p>nas nye ba'i snying po 'bum bzlas na de 'chi ba'i tshe ro lag tu byin nas mi 'khrugs pa'i zhing khams su skye'o/ /de nas dben pa'i gnas su khyer nas bdud rtsi'i bsgrub pa byas na dngos grub thams cad 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /skye ba bdun skra dang dud 'gro'i spu bsres nas srad bu byas nas
<p>229b.7</p>mgul du bcings na de'i gzugs su 'gyur ro zhes bya ba nas/ de'i gi wang zos na lus 'dir rang dang lhan cig tu khams gsum gyi rgyal por 'gyur ro zhes bya ba las tshogs lnga bcu pa yin no/ /le'u drug cu rtsa drug pa'i 'grel pa'o// //rtsa ba'i rgyud rnams las zhi khro tshang bar 'gyur
<p>230a</p>
<p>230a.1</p>ba'i phyir/ zhi ba'i lha gang dang gang yin shes par bya ba dang de la mos pa'i ched du zhi ba sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i dkyil 'khor ston pa ni/ de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ gong du bstan pa'i cho gas sngon 'gro lnga dang / 'byung ba bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rjer
<p>230a.2</p>gyur pa las gzhal yas khang gi dbus su rang gi chos kyi dbyings kyi yi ge las drod gsher skyes kyi lha bdag med pa'i chos kyi snang ba bsgom mo/ /de ltar mdor bstan nas rgyas par bshad pa ni/ rang gi chos kyi yi ge hUM las ye shes las skyes pa'i chos kyi lus su 'gyur/ he
<p>230a.3</p>las ni 'bras bu'i he ru kar bsgom mo/ /hi las tshogs pa bsgom mo/ hUM las srung ba'i 'khor lo'i tshe rdo rje hUM mdzad du bsgom mo/ /hUM las ni tshogs sogs pa'i lha mi bskyod pa bsgom mo/ /baM las ni gtso bo rdo rje sems dpa' bsgom mo/ /shar sangs rgyas mkha' 'gro/ /sku gsung
<p>230a.4</p>thugs ye shes kyi yi ge dang bzhi las skyes so/ /lhor rin chen mkha' 'gro yang yi ge bzhi las skyes/ nub pad+ma'i mkha' 'gro yang yi ge bzhi las skyes/ byang las kyi mkha' 'gro yang sku gsung thugs ye shes bzhi las skyes so/ /yum lnga ni ming mtshan gyi dang po yi ge re re las
<p>230a.5</p>skyes so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyi sku gsung thugs kyi yi ge he ru ka dang / maM bzhi las skyes so/ /thod pa'i dum bu la sogs pa sgyu 'phrul dra ba dang sbyar na 'jam pa'i rdo rje la sogs pa'i sems dpa'i ming ni go sla'o/ /lha mo rab gtum ma la sogs pa rdo rje pho nya mo zhes bya ba nas rdo rje 'jigs pa zhes bya
<p>230a.6</p>ba'i bar du sngon grub pa'i dpa' bo dang / lha mo'i oM bar du ming tha mar hUM phaT swA hA dang bcas pa snying po de nyid kyis dngos grub stsol lo/ /khwa gdong ma la sogs pa brgyad ni gshin rje gshed la sogs pa'i khro bo brgyad yin te/ dkar mo la sogs pa'i lha mo brgyad dang gnyis su med pa sgo dang
<p>230a.7</p>mtshams kha sbyar gyis gzhug pa thog mar oM bar du ming tha mar hUM phaT swA hA dang bcas pa'i snying po yin no/ /mtshams kyi gzugs rdo rje mas shar lho'i bum pa gzung / sgra rdo rje mas lho nub kyi bum pa gzung / dri rdo rje mas nub byang gi bum pa gzung / ro rdo rje mas byang shar gyi bum pa gzung / 
<p>230b</p>
<p>230b.1</p>reg rdo rje mas gtso bo rdo rje sems dpa' gzung / yum chos kyi dbyings lngas thabs ye shes lnga gzung ba yin no/ /las kyi rgyal mchog ni go cha bskon ye shes sems dpa' gzhug/ /dbang bskur bdud rtsi myang / bsgom pa dang bzlas pa bya'o/ /de'i don ni/ ye shes sems dpa'
<p>230b.2</p>gnyis med gzhug/ /rnal 'byor rgyud kyi rjes 'brangs nas/ /rnal 'byor ma dbang rtogs par bya/ /zhes pa yin no/ /rgyud 'bum pa rig pa'i rgya mtsho zhes grags pa de la dpa' bo rnams rgyas par bshad pa/ rtsa ba'i rgyud 'dir bsdus pa yin no/ /gzhung lugs sna tshogs bzang po 'di la bshad
<p>230b.3</p>pa'i rgyud bzhi yod de/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang sgyu ma bde mchog dang / rnal 'byor ma 'byung ba'i rgyud dang gsang ba'i rgyud do/ /nges brjod bla ma rgyud de dag gis rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi man ngag sems can bsam pa'i khyad par gang la mos pa rjes su gzung ba'i phyir/ gzhung lugs sna tshogs kyi man
<p>230b.4</p>ngag gis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub ster ro/ /dbus kyi 'khor lo la rigs lnga yab yum bcu thugs rdo rje phreng bas bskor/ gsung pad+ma'i phreng bas bskor/ sku 'khor lo'i phreng bas bskor ba'i rigs lnga dang byang chub sems dpa' du ma dang / khro bo brgyad dang / dkar mo la sogs pa
<p>230b.5</p>brgyad kyis phyogs skyong brgyad mnan nas 'khor gyi mchog dang sgo dang mtshams su dgod par bya'o/ /sku mdog dang phyag mtshan rgyud na gsal bas go sla'o/ /nyan thos dang rang rgyal ba'i sangs rgyas dang mu stegs can la gsang ba dang / mchod pa dang bstod pa gtor ma gtang ba bla ma'i
<p>230b.6</p>zhal nas sam/ rmi lam du rnal 'byor ma'i drin gyis bstan nas/ lha rnams kyi rnam dag sum cu rtsa drug bsgom pa dang / gnas bcu sa bcu dang / pha rol tu phyin pa bcu rtogs pa dang / dang po sbyor ba dkyil 'khor rgyal mchog las rgyal mchog gi sbyor ba gsum/ rnam par dag
<p>230b.7</p>pa'i don dri ma med pa'i mchog bsgom pa ni mjug gi sdom pa yin no/ /le'u drug cu rtsa bdun pa'i 'grel pa'o// //da ni/ rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor mchog tu bshad bya ba/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ bdag nyid bsgom pa'i go cha'i rim pa zhes bya ba ni/ sngon 'gro lnga dang 'byung ba
<p>231a</p>
<p>231a.1</p>bzhi ri rab sna tshogs rdo rjer gyur pa las gzhal yas khang de'i nang du so sor 'brang ma'i gzungs las 'byung ba bzhin du/ gtso bo zhal lnga pa phyag sum cu rtsa gnyis la/ 'khor gyi lha mo mA ma kI dang / spyan ma dang / sgrol ma dang / gos dkar mo dang / 'od zer can
<p>231a.2</p>dang / rmug 'dzin ma dang / skul byed ma dang / sa 'dzin ma dang brgyad ni zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa gtso bo rdo rje'i skyil mo krung / 'khor sems dpa'i skyil mo krung gis bzhugs par bsgom mo/ /yang na rang gi ming las byung ba'i khro bo brgyad shar sngo lho ser/ nub dmar byang ljang / 
<p>231a.3</p>shar lho gnag /lho nub dkar/ /nub byang ser/ byang shar sngo ba sna tshogs pa'i gzugs can ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa khro ba'i mchog 'byung po 'dul byed ni dbus su mig sman sngon po'i mdog can rdo rje dang sdigs mdzub na bza' sngon po stag gi pags pa'i sham thabs can
<p>231a.4</p>sbrul gyis brgyan pa mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i tshe yang zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa bsgom par bya'o/ /phra ba nang gi rdo rje can bsgom pa ni snying ga'i nu ma'i bar du khro bo dgu/ gnas gsum du 'khor lo gsum gyi lhas 'gro ba gsum po dag par byas pa ni mchod pa dang po'o/ /gang gi rdo
<p>231a.5</p>rje'i sbyor bas 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga'i rdo rjes mchod pa ni gnyis pa'o/ /mchod pa lnga me tog dang bdug pa la sogs pas mchod pa ni gsum pa'o/ /stong pa nyid bzhi yum bzhi mnyam pa nyid kyi mchod pa ni bzhi pa'o/ /ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / go cha bgo ba dang / 
<p>231a.6</p>dbang bskur ba dang / bdud rtsi myang ba dang / gtor ma gtang ba ni kha bskang ngo / /le'u drug cu rtsa brgyad pa'i 'grel pa'o// //lha'i 'khor lo sngar bshad pa rgyud 'bum pa las sngags dang de nyid rgyas par bstan/ rgyud 'dir mdor bstan pa'i lha'i 'khor lo ni don dam pa ma
<p>231a.7</p>yin/ gal te don dam pa'i shes pa skyes na ston pa po dang bstan pa lha'i 'khor lo yang med do/ /'o na su'i don du bstan zhe na/ 'khor ba 'dir sgyu ma sdug bsngal can gyis skyes pa la lha nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i 'khor lo gnas dang bcas pa sgyu ma can bstan pa don dam pa'i bden par
<p>231b</p>
<p>231b.1</p>ni ma yin no/ /gal te don dam par med na lha'i 'khor lo 'khrul pas ci zhig bya/ 'on te don dam pa'i ye shes la rnam pa lha'i 'khor lo yod na 'khrul pa ci yod ce na/ gnas dang nye ba'i gnas la sogs pas sgyu ma sdug bsngal can spangs nas sgyu ma bde ba dri ma med par 'gyur ro/ /
<p>231b.2</p>yang don dam pa'i bsgom pa mi nus pa 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la bag med par spyod pa'i mi la thams cad lha'i 'khor lo byas nas gnas 'di bsgrags par bya'o/ /ngas dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo du ma bshad pa ni/ sems can bsam pa sna tshogs yod pas bsam gtan gyi bde bar
<p>231b.3</p>bsgom pa'i phyir lha'i 'khor lo bshad do/ /rnal 'byor pa phyi rol gyi zhing rmo ba dang / tshong bya ba dang / phyugs bskyang ba dang / spyod lam rnam bzhi sdug bsngal bas khams zad par 'gyur ba la de spangs nas snod kyi 'jig rten gzhal yas khang 'gro ba rigs drug lha'i 'khor lo 'dod pa'i
<p>231b.4</p>yon tan lngas mchod pa'i rol pas gnas pa'i rnal 'byor can/ de la sangs rgyas kyi spyan lngas gzigs nas ci 'dod pa'i dngos grub mtha' yas pa'i dngos grub stsol lo/ /don dam par med kyang kun rdzob tu bsod nams kyi tshogs bsgom pa bshad nas/ brtan pa thob pa'i
<p>231b.5</p>rnal 'byor pa des rje btsun gyi ye shes la 'bad de bsgrub par bya'o/ /ji ltar bya zhe na/ lha sna tshogs kyi mdzad pa dang ldan pa'i lus po lha'i cha byad bya/ gang yang rung ba'i kha zas bdud rtsir bsam/ nyal ba gcer bu'am ma nyal ba gos dang bcas pa rang gi lha'i rnam pa'i
<p>231b.6</p>nga rgyal bya/ lkugs pa bzhin du mi smra bar bzlas pa byas na zla drug gis lha gang 'dod pa gsal bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi spyod pa dang brtul zhugs bshad nas/ phan yon gyi mngon par shes pa skyes nas pad+ma'i rdzing bu lta bu'i rnal 'byor pa la dpa'
<p>231b.7</p>bo dang rnal 'byor ma rnams ngang pa'i tshogs bzhin du 'du ba dang / yid mig 'phrul mkhan sgyu mkhan ltar 'gro ba'i don byed pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa 'khor dang bcas pa mngon sum du mthong bar the tshom med do/ /phan yon bshad nas/ gdams ngag ston pa ni mngon par 'dod pa'i
<p>232a</p>
<p>232a.1</p>dkyil 'khor 'di la nges par sna gtad nas dad pa skad cig tsam bshad pa nyan pas sems dga' bar gyis shig ces gsol ba 'debs so/ /dkyil 'khor lnga bcu rtsa drug gi thams cad ldan pa'i tshe rdo rje drag po hUM mdzad kyi sbyor ba dang ldan pa'i snying gar sngags
<p>232a.2</p>bkod pa la 'od zer lcags kyu lta bu'i sbyor bas lus kyi dkyil 'khor sngags la bsdus nas sngags chos kyi dbyings sems kyi 'khor lo chos kyi dbyings su brtag go/ /rang gi chos kyi yi ge go cha drug gis skye mched drug gzung 'dzin dang bral bar bsgom mo/ /ji ltar lha'i 'khor
<p>232a.3</p>lo rtag pa'i snying gar bsdus nas/ thun mtshams su zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa gzhan gyi gzugs su bsgom par bya'o/ /sems yid gti mug pa mos pa mtha' yas pa la gzugs sna tshogs su bstan par blta bar bya'o/ /le'u drug cu rtsa dgu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //
<p>232a.4</p>rang bzhin med pa'i chos rnams zhes pa'i tshigs bcad gcig ni rgyud brjod bya'o/ /rgyud rdzogs pa yis sbyor ba yin/ /zhes pa tshigs bcad gcig gis ni rgyu'i rgyud la rjes su yi rangs shing bstod pa'o/ /sangs rgyas byang chub dka' drin mchog /ces pa'i tshigs bcad phyed ni
<p>232a.5</p>thabs kyi rgyud la bstod pa'o/ /sgrub pa'i bla ma'i bla ma ste/ /zhes pa'i tshigs bcad gnyis ni 'bras bu'i rgyud la bstod pa'o/ /legs so rdo rje'i bla ma kun/ /zhes pa tshigs bcad gcig gis rgyud 'bum pa 'chad pa'i gtso bo dang 'khor la bstod pa'o/ /le'u bdun cu pa'i 'grel pa'o// //
<p>232a.6</p>rtsa ba'i rgyud chen po man ngag thams cad mngon zhing nges par brjod pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon shU raM ga badzras mdzad pa rdzogs so// //bcom ldan 'das bde mchog gi rgyud 'bum pa chen po'i gdams ngag de kho na nyid tshang bar bsdus pa man ngag thams cad kyi snying po nges
<p>232a.7</p>par brjod pa'i rgyud bla ma'i yang bla ma zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa/ bde mchog 'bum pa'i de kho na nyid nges par byed pa de kho na nyid kyi snying po zhes bya ba sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po 'phags pa shes rab kyis dz+nyA na shrI mi tra'i gsung ji lta ba bzhin du bsgyur ba'o// //
